atha vakṣyāmi śaivānāmihaiva phaladaṃ nṛṇām /
pūjāhomajapadhyānatapodānamayaṃ mahat // 7.2,32.2 //
tatra saṃsādhayetpūrvaṃ mantraṃ mantrārthavittamaḥ /
dṛṣṭasiddhikaraṃ karma nānyathā phaladaṃ yataḥ // 7.2,32.3 //
siddhamantro 'pyadṛṣṭena prabalena tu kenacit /
pratibandhaphalaṃ karma na kuryātsahasā budhaḥ // 7.2,32.4 //
tasya tu pratibandhasya kartuṃ śakyeha niṣkṛtiḥ /
parīkṣya śakunādyaistadādau niṣkṛtimācaret // 7.2,32.5 //
yo 'nyathā kurute mohātkarmaihikaphalaṃ naraḥ /
na tena phalabhāksa syātprāpnuyāccopahāsyatām // 7.2,32.6 //
abisrabdho na kurvīta karma dṛṣṭaphalaṃ kvacit /
sa khalvaśraddhadhānaḥ syānnāśraddhaḥ phalamṛcchati // 7.2,32.7 //
nāparādhosti devasya karmaṇyapi tu niṣphale /
yathoktakāriṇāṃ puṃsāmihaiva phaladarśanāt // 7.2,32.8 //
sādhakaḥ siddhamaṃtraśca nirastapratibaṃdhakaḥ /
viśvastaḥ śraddhadhānaśca kurvannāpnoti tatphalam // 7.2,32.9 //
athavā tatphalāvāptyai brahmacaryarato bhavet /
rātrau haviṣyamaśnīyātpāyasaṃ vā phalāni vā // 7.2,32.10 //
hiṃsādi yanniṣiddhaṃ syānna kuryānmanasāpi tat /
sadā bhasmānuliptāṃ gassuveṣaśca śucirbhavet // 7.2,32.11 //
itthamācāravānbhūtvā svānukūle śubhe 'hani /
pūrvoktalakṣaṇe deśe puṣpadāmādyalaṃkṛte // 7.2,32.12 //
ālipya śakṛtā bhūmiṃ hastamānāvarāṃ yathā /
vilikhetkamale bhadre dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā // 7.2,32.13 //
taptajāṃbūnadamayamaṣṭapatraṃ sakesaram /
madhye karṇikayā yuktaṃ sarvaratnairalaṃkṛtam // 7.2,32.14 //
svākārasadṛśenaiva nālena ca samanvitam /
tādṛśe svarṇanirmāṇe kaṃde samyagvidhānataḥ // 7.2,32.15 //
tatrāṇimādikaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkalpya manasā punaḥ /
ratnajaṃ vātha sauvarṇaṃ sphaṭikaṃ vā salakṣaṇam /
liṅgaṃ savedikaṃ caiva sthāpayitvā vidhānataḥ // 7.2,32.16 //
tatrāvāhya yajeddevaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyayam /
tatra māheśvarī kalpyā mūrtirmūrtimataḥ prabhoḥ // 7.2,32.17 //
caturbhujā caturvaktrā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā /
śārdūlacarmavasanā kiṃcidvihasitānanā // 7.2,32.18 //
varadābhayahastā ca mṛgaṭaṃkadharā tathā /
atha vāṣṭabhujā ciṃtyā ciṃtakasya yathāruci // 7.2,32.19 //
tadā triśūlaparaśukhaḍgavajrāṇi dakṣiṇe /
vāme pāśāṃkuśau tadvatkheṭaṃ nāgaṃ ca bibhratī // 7.2,32.20 //
bālārkasadṛśaprakhyā prativaktraṃ trilocanā /
tasyāḥ pūrvamukhaṃ saumyaṃ svākārasadṛśaprabham // 7.2,32.21 //
dakṣiṇaṃ nīlajīmūtasadṛśaṃ ghoradarśanam /
uttaraṃ vidrumaprakhyaṃ nīlālakavibhūṣitam // 7.2,32.22 //
paścimaṃ pūrṇacaṃdrābhaṃ saumyamiṃdukalādharam /
tadaṃkamaṃḍalārūḍhā śaktirmāheśvarī parā // 7.2,32.23 //
mahālakṣmīriti khyātā śyāmā sarvamanoharā /
mūrtiṃ kṛtvaivamākārāṃ sakalīkṛtya ca kramāt // 7.2,32.24 //
mūrtimaṃtamathāvāhya yajetparamakāraṇam /
snānārthe kalpayettatra pañcagavyaṃ tu kāpilam // 7.2,32.25 //
pañcāmṛtaṃ ca pūrṇāni bījāni ca viśeṣataḥ /
purastānmaṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā ratnacūrṇādyalaṃkṛtam // 7.2,32.26 //
karṇikāyāṃ pravinyasyedīśānakalaśaṃ punaḥ /
sadyādikalaśānpaścātparitastasya kalpayet // 7.2,32.27 //
tato vidyeśakalaśānaṣṭau pūrvādivatkramāt /
tīrthāmbupūritānkṛtvā sūtreṇāveṣṭya pūrvavat // 7.2,32.28 //
puṇyadravyāṇi nikṣipya samantraṃ savidhānakam /
dukūlādyena vastreṇa samācchādya samaṃtataḥ // 7.2,32.29 //
sarvatra maṃtraṃ vinyasya tattanmaṃtrapurassaram /
snānakāle tu saṃprāpte sarvamaṅgalanisvanaiḥ // 7.2,32.30 //
pañcagavyādibhiścaiva snāpayetparameśvaram /
tataḥ kuśodakādyāni svarṇaratnodakānyapi // 7.2,32.31 //
gaṃdhapuṣpādisiddhāni mantrasiddhāni ca kramāt /
uddhṛtyoddhṛtya mantreṇa taistaissnāpya maheśvaram // 7.2,32.32 //
gaṃdhaṃ puṣpādidīpāṃśca pūjākarma samācaret /
palāvaraḥ syādālepa ekādaśapalottaraḥ // 7.2,32.33 //
suvarṇaratnapuṣpāṇi śubhāni surabhīṇi ca /
nīlotpalādyutpalāni bilvapatrāṇyanekaśaḥ // 7.2,32.34 //
kamalāni ca raktāni śvetānyapi ca śaṃbhave /
kṛṣṇāgurūdbhavo dhūpaḥ sakarpūrājyaguggulaḥ // 7.2,32.35 //
kapilāghṛtasaṃsiddhā dīpāḥ karpūravartijāḥ /
pañcabrahmaṣaḍaṃgāni pūjyānyāvaraṇāni ca // 7.2,32.36 //
naivedyaḥ payasā siddhaḥ sa guḍājyo mahācaruḥ /
pāṭalotpalapadmādyaiḥ pānīyaṃ ca sugandhitam // 7.2,32.37 //
pañcasaugaṃdhikopetaṃ tāṃbūlaṃ ca susaṃskṛtam /
suvarṇaratnasiddhāni bhūṣaṇāni viśeṣataḥ // 7.2,32.38 //
vāsāṃsi ca vicitrāṇi sūkṣmāṇi ca navāni ca /
darśanīyāni deyāni gānavādyādibhissaha // 7.2,32.39 //
japaśca mūlamaṃtrasya lakṣaḥ paramasaṃkhyayā /
ekāvarā tryuttarā ca pūjā phalavaśādiha // 7.2,32.40 //
daśasaṃkhyāvaro homaḥ pratidravyaṃ śatottaraḥ /
ghorarūpaśśivaściṃtyo māraṇoccāṭanādiṣu // 7.2,32.41 //
śivaliṃge śivāgnau ca hyanyāsu pratimāsu ca /
ciṃtyassaumyatanuśśaṃbhuḥ kārye śāṃtikapauṣṭike // 7.2,32.42 //
āyasau sruksruvau kāryau māraṇādiṣu karmasu /
tadanyatra tu sauvarṇau śāṃtikādyeṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ // 7.2,32.43 //
dūrvayā ghṛtagokṣīramiśrayā madhunā tathā /
caruṇā saghṛtenaiva kevalaṃ payasāpi vā // 7.2,32.44 //
juhuyānmṛtyuvijaye tilai rogopaśāṃtaye /
ghṛtena payasā caiva kamalairvātha kevalaiḥ // 7.2,32.45 //
samṛddhikāmo juhuyānmahādāridryaśāṃtaye /
jātīpuṣpeṇa vaśyārthī juhuyātsaghṛtena tu // 7.2,32.46 //
ghṛtena karavīraiśca kuryādākarṣaṇaṃ dvijaḥ /
tailenoccāṭanaṃ kuryātstaṃbhanaṃ madhunā punaḥ // 7.2,32.47 //
staṃbhanaṃ sarṣapeṇāpi laśunena tu pātanam /
tāḍanaṃ rudhireṇa syātkharasyoṣṭrasya cobhayoḥ // 7.2,32.48 //
māraṇoccāṭane kuryādrohibījaistilānvitaiḥ /
vidveṣaṇaṃ ca tailena kuryāllāṃgalakasya tu // 7.2,32.49 //
baṃdhanaṃ rohibījena senāstaṃbhanameva ca /
raktasarṣapasaṃmiśrairhomadravyairaśeṣataḥ // 7.2,32.50 //
hastayaṃtrodbhavaistailairjuhuyādābhicārike /
kaṭukītuṣasaṃyuktaiḥ kārpāsāsthibhireva ca // 7.2,32.51 //
sarṣapaistailasaṃmiśrairjuhuyādābhicārike /
jvaropaśāṃtidaṃ kṣīraṃ saubhāgyaphaladaṃ tathā // 7.2,32.52 //
sarvasiddhikaro homaḥ kṣaudrājyadadhibhiryutaiḥ /
kṣīreṇa taṃdulaiścaiva caruṇā kevalena vā // 7.2,32.53 //
śāṃtikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ vāpi saptabhiḥ samidādibhiḥ /
dravyairviśeṣato home vaśyamākarṣaṇaṃ tathā // 7.2,32.54 //
vaśyamākarṣaṇaṃ caiva śrīpadaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ /
bilvapatraistu havanaṃ śatrorvijayadaṃ tathā // 7.2,32.55 //
samidhaḥ śāṃtikāryeṣu pālāśakhadirādikāḥ /
karavīrārkajāḥ kraurye kaṇṭakinyaśca vigrahe // 7.2,32.56 //
praśāṃtaḥ śāṃtikaṃ kuryātpauṣṭikaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ /
nirghṛṇaḥ kruddhacittastu prakuryādābhicārikam // 7.2,32.57 //
atīvaduravasthāyāṃ pratīkārāṃtaraṃ na cet /
ātatāyinamuddiśya prakuryādābhicārikam // 7.2,32.58 //
svarāṣṭrapatimuddiśya na kuryādābhicārikam /
yadyāstikassudharmiṣṭho mānyo vā yo 'pi kopi vā // 7.2,32.59 //
tamuddiśyāpi no kuryādātatāyinamapyuta /
manasā karmaṇā vācā yo 'pi kopi śivāśritaḥ // 7.2,32.60 //
svarāṣṭrapatimuddiśya śivā śritamathāpi vā /
kṛtvābhicārikaṃ karma sadyo vinipatennaraḥ // 7.2,32.61 //
svarāṣṭrapālakaṃ tasmācchivabhaktaṃ ca kañcana /
na hiṃsyādabhicārādyairyadīcchetsukhamātmanaḥ // 7.2,32.62 //
anyaṃ kamapi coddiśya kṛtvā vai māraṇādikam /
paścāttāpena saṃyuktaḥ prāyaścittaṃ samācaret // 7.2,32.63 //
bāṇaliṃge 'pi vā kuryānnirdhano dhanavānapi /
svayaṃbhūte 'tha vā liṃge ārṣake vaidike 'pi vā // 7.2,32.64 //
abhāve hemaratnānāmaśaktau ca tadarjane /
manasaivācaredetaddravyairvā pratirūpakaiḥ // 7.2,32.65 //
kvacidaṃśe tu yaḥ śaktastvaśaktaḥ kvacidaṃśake /
so 'pi śaktyanusāreṇa kurvaṃścetphalamṛcchati // 7.2,32.66 //
karmaṇyanuṣṭhite 'pyasminphalaṃ yatra na dṛśyate /
dvistrirvāvartayettatra sarvathā dṛśyate phalam // 7.2,32.67 //
pūjopayuktaṃ yaddravyaṃ hemaratnādyanuttamam /
tatsarvaṃ gurave dadyāddakṣiṇāṃ ca tataḥ pṛthak // 7.2,32.68 //
sa cennecchati tatsarvaṃ śivāya vinivedayet /
athavā śivabhaktebhyo nānyebhyastu pradīyate // 7.2,32.69 //
yaḥ svayaṃ sādhayecchaktyā gurvādinirapekṣayā /
so 'pyevamācaredatra na gṛhṇīyātsvayaṃ punaḥ // 7.2,32.70 //
svayaṃ gṛhṇāti yo lobhātpūjāṃgadravyamuttamam /
kāṃkṣitaṃ na labhenmūḍho nātra kāryā vicāraṇā // 7.2,32.71 //
arcitaṃ yattu talliṃgaṃ gṛhṇīyādvā navā svayam /
gṛhṇīyādyadi tannityaṃ svayaṃ vānyo 'pi vārcayet // 7.2,32.72 //
yathoktameva karmaitadācaredyo 'napāyataḥ /
phalaṃ vyabhicarennaivamityataḥ kiṃ prarocakam // 7.2,32.73 //
tathāpyuddeśato vakṣye karmaṇaḥ siddhimuttamam /
api śatrubhirākrāṃto vyādhibhirvāpyanekaśaḥ // 7.2,32.74 //
mṛtyorāsyagataścāpi mucyate nirapāyataḥ /
pūjāyate 'tikṛpaṇo rikto vaiśravaṇāyate // 7.2,32.75 //
kāmāyate virūpo 'pi vṛddho 'pi taruṇāyate /
śatrurmitrāyate sadyo virodhī kiṃkarāyate // 7.2,32.76 //
viṣāyate yadamṛtaṃ viṣamapyamṛtāyate /
sthalāyate samudro 'pi sthalamapyarṇavāyate // 7.2,32.77 //
mahīdharāyate śvabhraṃ sa ca śvabhrāyate giriḥ /
padmākarāyate vahniḥ saro vaiśvānarāyate // 7.2,32.78 //
vanāyate yadudyānaṃ tadudyānāyate vanam /
siṃhāyate mṛgaḥ kṣudraḥ siṃhaḥ krīḍāmṛgāyate // 7.2,32.79 //
striyo 'bhisārikāyante lakṣmīḥ sucaritāyate /
svairapreṣyāyate vāṇī kīrtistu gaṇikāyate // 7.2,32.80 //
svairācārāyate medhā vajrasūcīyate manaḥ /
mahāvātāyate śaktirbalaṃ mattagajāyate // 7.2,32.81 //
stambhāyate samudyogaiḥ śatrupakṣe sthitā kriyā /
śatrupakṣāyate 'rīṇāṃ sarva eva suhṛjjanaḥ // 7.2,32.82 //
śatravaḥ kuṇapāyante jīvantopi sabāṃdhavāḥ /
āpanno 'pi gatāriṣṭaḥ svayaṃ khalvamṛtāyate // 7.2,32.83 //
rasāya nāyate nityamapathyamapi sevitam /
aniśaṃ kriyamāṇāpi ratistvabhinavāyate // 7.2,32.84 //
anāgatādikaṃ sarvaṃ karasthāmalakāyate /
yādṛcchikaphalāyante siddhayo 'pyaṇimādayaḥ // 7.2,32.85 //
bahunātra kimuktena sarvakāmārthasiddhiṣu /
asminkarmaṇi nirvṛtte tvanavāpyaṃ na vidyate // 7.2,32.86 //
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe aihikasiddhikarmavarṇanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
upamanyuruvāca /
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kevalāmuṣmikaṃ vidhim /
naitena sadṛśaṃ kiṃcitkarmāsti bhuvanatraye // 7.2,33.1 //
puṇyātiśayasaṃyuktaḥ sarvairdevairanuṣṭhitaḥ /
brahmaṇā viṣṇunā caiva rudreṇa ca viśeṣataḥ // 7.2,33.2 //
iṃdrādilokapāraiśca sūryādyairnavabhirgrahaiḥ /
viśvāmitravasiṣṭhādyairbrahmavidbhirmaharṣibhiḥ // 7.2,33.3 //
śvetāgastyadadhīcādyairasmābhiśca śivāśritaiḥ /
naṃdīśvaramahākālabhṛṃgīśādyairgaṇeśvaraiḥ // 7.2,33.4 //
pātālavāsibhirdaityaiḥ śeṣādyaiśca mahoragaiḥ /
siddhairyakṣaiśca gaṃdharvai rakṣobhūtapiśācakaiḥ // 7.2,33.5 //
svaṃsvaṃ padamanuprāptaṃ sarvairayamanuṣṭhitaḥ /
anena vidhinā sarve devā devatvamāgatāḥ // 7.2,33.6 //
brahmā brahmatvamāpanno viṣṇurviṣṇutvamāgataḥ /
rudro rudratvamāpanna iṃdraścendratvamāgataḥ // 7.2,33.7 //
gaṇeśaśca gaṇeśatvamanena vidhinā gataḥ /
sitacaṃdanatoyena liṃgaṃ snāpya śivaṃ śivām /
śvetairvikasitaiḥ padmaiḥ saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca // 7.2,33.8 //
tatra padmāsanaṃ ramyaṃ kṛtvā lakṣaṇasaṃyutam /
vibhave sati hemādyai ratnādyairvā svaśaktitaḥ // 7.2,33.9 //
madhye kesarajālāsya sthāpya liṃgaṃ kanīyasam /
aṃguṣṭhapratimaṃ ramyaṃ sarvagandhamayaṃ śubham // 7.2,33.10 //
dakṣiṇe sthāpayitvā tu bilvapatraiḥ samarcayet /
aguruṃ dakṣiṇe pārśve paścime tu manaḥśilām // 7.2,33.11 //
uttare caṃdanaṃ dadyāddharitālaṃ tu pūrvataḥ /
sugandhaiḥ kusumai ramyairvicitraiścāpi pūjayet // 7.2,33.12 //
dhūpaṃ kṛṣṇāguruṃ dadyātsarvataśca saguggulam /
vāsāṃsi cātisūkṣmāṇi vikāśāni nivedayet // 7.2,33.13 //
pāyasaṃ ghṛtasaṃmiśraṃ ghṛtadīpāṃśca dāpayet /
sarvaṃ nivedya mantreṇa tato gacchetpradakṣiṇām // 7.2,33.14 //
praṇamya bhaktyā deveśaṃ stutvā cānte kṣamāpayet /
sarvopahārasaṃmiśraṃ tato liṃgaṃ nivedayet // 7.2,33.15 //
śivāya śivamantreṇa dakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ /
evaṃ yo 'rcayate nityaṃ pañcagandhamayaṃ śubham // 7.2,33.16 //
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivaloke mahīyate /
etadvratottamaṃ guhyaṃ śivaliṃgamahāvratam // 7.2,33.17 //
bhaktasya te samākhyātaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit /
deyaṃ ca śivabhaktebhyaḥ śivena kathitaṃ purā // 7.2,33.18 //
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe āmuṣmikakarmavidhivarṇanaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
upamanyuruvāca /
nityanaimittikātkāmyādyā siddhiriha kīrtitā /
sā sarvā labhyeta sadyo liṃgaberapratiṣṭhayā // 7.2,34.1 //
sarvo liṃgamayo lokassarvaṃ liṃge pratiṣṭhitam /
tasmātpratiṣṭhite liṃge bhavetsarvaṃ patiṣṭhitam // 7.2,34.2 //
brahmaṇā viṣṇunā vāpi rudreṇānyena kena vā /
liṃgapratiṣṭhāmutsṛjya kriyate svapadasthitiḥ // 7.2,34.3 //
kimanyadiha vaktavyaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ prati kāraṇam /
partiṣṭhitaṃ śivenāpi liṃgaṃ vaiśveśvaraṃ yataḥ // 7.2,34.4 //
tasmātsarvaprayatnena paratreha ca śarmaṇe /
sthāpayetparameśasya liṃgaṃ beramathāpi vā // 7.2,34.5 //
śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca /
kimidaṃ liṃgamākhyātaṃ kathaṃ liṃgī maheśvaraḥ /
kathaṃ ca liṃgabhāvo 'sya kasmādasmiñchivo 'rcyate // 7.2,34.6 //
upamanyuruvāca /
avyaktaṃ liṃgamākhyātaṃ triguṇaprabhavāpyayam /
anādyanaṃtaṃ viśvasya yadupādānakāraṇam // 7.2,34.7 //
tadeva mūlaprakṛtirmāyā ca gaganātmikā /
tata eva samutpannaṃ jagadetaccarācaram // 7.2,34.8 //
aśuddhaṃ caiva śuddhaṃ yacchuddhāśuddhaṃ ca tattridhā /
tataḥ śivo maheśaśca rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ // 7.2,34.9 //
bhūtāni cendriyairjātā līyante 'tra śivājñayā /
ata eva śivo liṃgo liṃgamājñāpayedyataḥ // 7.2,34.10 //
yato na tadanājñātaṃ kāryāya prabhavetsvataḥ /
tato jātasya viśvasya tatraiva vilayo yataḥ // 7.2,34.11 //
anena liṃgatāṃ tasya bhavennānyena kenacit /
liṃgaṃ ca śivayordehastābhyāṃ yasmādadhiṣṭhitam // 7.2,34.12 //
atastatra śivaḥ sāmbo nityameva samarcayet /
liṃgavedī mahādevī liṃgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ // 7.2,34.13 //
tayoḥ saṃpūjanādeva sa ca sā ca samarcitau /
na tayorliṃgadehatvaṃ vidyate paramārthataḥ // 7.2,34.14 //
yatastvetau viśuddhau tau dehastadupacārataḥ /
tadeva paramā śaktiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ // 7.2,34.15 //
śaktirājñāṃ yadādatte prasūte taccarācaram /
na tasya mahimā śakyo vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi // 7.2,34.16 //
yenādau mohitau syātāṃ brahmanārāyaṇāvapi /
purā tribhuvanasyāsya pralaye samupasthite // 7.2,34.17 //
vāriśayyāgato viṣṇuḥ suṣvāpānākulaḥ sukham /
yadṛcchayā gatastatra brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ // 7.2,34.18 //
dadarśa puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ svapantaṃ tamanākulam /
māyayā mohitaḥ śambhorviṣṇumāha pitāmahaḥ // 7.2,34.19 //
kastvaṃ vadetyamarṣeṇa prahṛtyotthāpya mādhavam /
sa tu hastaprahāreṇa tīvreṇābhihataḥ kṣaṇāt // 7.2,34.20 //
prabuddhotthāya śayanāddadarśa parameṣṭhinam /
tamāha cāṃtassaṃkruddhaḥ svayamakruddhavaddhariḥ // 7.2,34.21 //
kutastvamāgato vatsa kasmāttvaṃ vyākulo vada /
iti viṣṇuvacaḥ śrutvā prabhutvaguṇasūcakam // 7.2,34.22 //
rajasā baddhavairastaṃ brahmā punarabhāṣata /
vatseti māṃ kuto brūṣe guruḥ śiṣyamivātmanaḥ // 7.2,34.23 //
māṃ na jānāsi kiṃ nāthaṃ prapañco yasya me kṛtiḥ /
tridhātmānaṃ vibhajyedaṃ sṛṣṭvātha paripālyate // 7.2,34.24 //
saṃharāmi name kaścitsraṣṭā jagati vidyate /
ityukte sati so 'pyāha brahmāṇaṃ viṣṇuravyayaḥ // 7.2,34.25 //
ahamevādikartāsya hartā ca paripālakaḥ /
bhavānapi mamaivāṃgādavatīrṇaḥ purāvyayāt // 7.2,34.26 //
manniyogāttvamātmānaṃ tridhā kṛtvā jagattrayam /
sṛjasyavasi cāṃte tatpunaḥ pratisṛjasyapi // 7.2,34.27 //
vismṛtosi jagannāthaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam /
tavāpi janakaṃ sākṣānmāmevamavamanyase // 7.2,34.28 //
tavāparādho nāstyatra bhrāṃtosi mama māyayā /
matprasādādiyaṃ bhrāṃtirapaiṣyati tavācirāt // 7.2,34.29 //
śṛṇu satyaṃ caturvaktra sarvadeveśvaro hyaham /
kartā bhartā ca hartā ca na mayāsti samo vibhuḥ // 7.2,34.30 //
evameva vivādobhūdbrahmaviṣṇvoḥ parasparam /
abhavacca mahāyuddhaṃ bhairavaṃ romaharṣaṇam // 7.2,34.31 //
muṣṭibhirnnighnatostīvraṃ rajasā baddhavairayoḥ /
tayordarpāpahārāya prabodhāya ca devayoḥ // 7.2,34.32 //
madhye samāvirabhavalliṃgamaiśvaramadbhutam /
jvālāmālāsahasrāḍhyamaprameyamanaupamam // 7.2,34.33 //
kṣayavṛddhivinirmuktamādimadhyāṃtavarjitam /
tasya jvālāsahasreṇa brahmaviṣṇū vimohitau // 7.2,34.34 //
visṛjya yuddhaṃ kiṃ tvetadityaciṃtayatāṃ tadā /
na tayostasya yāthātmyaṃ prabuddhamabhavadyadā // 7.2,34.35 //
tadā samudyatau syātāṃ tasyādyaṃtaṃ parīkṣitum /
tatra haṃsākṛtirbrahmā viśvataḥ pakṣasaṃyutaḥ /
manonilajavo bhūtvā gatastūrdhvaṃ prayatnataḥ // 7.2,34.37 //
nārāyaṇopi viśvātmā līlāñjanacayopamam /
vārāhamamitaṃ rūpamasthāya gatavānadhaḥ // 7.2,34.38 //
evaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tvaran viṣṇuradhogataḥ /
nāpaśyadalpamapyasya mūlaṃ liṃgasya sūkaraḥ // 7.2,34.39 //
tāvatkālaṃ gataścordhvaṃ tasyāṃtaṃ jñātumicchayā /
śrāṃtotyaṃtamadṛṣṭvāṃtaṃ pāpatādhaḥ pitāmahaḥ // 7.2,34.40 //
tathaiva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śrāṃtaḥ saṃvignalocanaḥ /
kleśena mahatā tūrṇamadhastādutthito 'bhavat // 7.2,34.41 //
samāgatāvathānyonyaṃ vismayasmeravīkṣaṇau /
māyayā mohitau śaṃbhoḥ kṛtyākṛtyaṃ na jagmatuḥ // 7.2,34.42 //
pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvatastasya cāgrataśca sthitāvubhau /
praṇipatya kimātmedamityaciṃtayatāṃ tadā // 7.2,34.43 //
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe harividhimohavarṇanaṃ nāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
upamanyuruvāca /
athāvirabhavattatra sanādaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam /
omityekākṣaraṃ brahma brahmaṇaḥ pratipādakam // 7.2,35.1 //
tadapyaviditaṃ tāvadbrahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā /
rajasā tamasā cittaṃ tayoryasmāttiraskṛtam // 7.2,35.2 //
tadā vibhaktamabhavaccaturdhaikaṃ tadakṣaram /
a u meti trimātrābhiḥ parastāccārdhamātrayā // 7.2,35.3 //
tatrākāraḥ śrito bhāge jvalalliṃgasya dakṣiṇe /
ukāraścottare tadvanmakārastasya madhyataḥ // 7.2,35.4 //
ardhamātrātmako nādaḥ śrūyate liṃgamūrdhani /
vibhakte 'pi tadā tasminpraṇave paramākṣare // 7.2,35.5 //
vibhāvārthaṃ ca tau devau na kiṃcidavajagmatuḥ /
vedātmanā tadāvyaktaḥ praṇavo vikṛtiṃ gataḥ // 7.2,35.6 //
tatrākāro ṛgabhavadukāro yajuravyayaḥ /
makārassāma saṃjāto nādastvātharvaṇī śrutiḥ // 7.2,35.7 //
ṛgayaṃ sthāpayāmāsa samāsāttvarthamātmanaḥ /
rajoguṇeṣu brahmāṇaṃ mūrtiṣvādyaṃ kriyāsvapi // 7.2,35.8 //
sṛṣṭiṃ lokeṣu pṛthivīṃ tattveṣvātmānamavyayam /
kalādhvani nivṛttiṃ ca sadyaṃ brahmasu pañcasu // 7.2,35.9 //
liṃgabhāgeṣvadhobhāgaṃ bījākhyaṃ kāraṇatraye /
catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaiśvaryaṃ bauddhaṃ yadaṇimādiṣu // 7.2,35.10 //
taditthamarthairdaśabhirvyāptaṃ viśvamṛcā jagat /
athopasthāpayāmāsa svārthaṃ daśavidhaṃ yajuḥ // 7.2,35.11 //
sattvaṃ guṇeṣu viṣṇuṃ ca mūrtiṣvādyaṃ kriyāsvapi /
sthitiṃ lokeṣvaṃtarikṣaṃ vidyāṃ tattveṣu ca triṣu // 7.2,35.12 //
kalādhvasu pratiṣṭhāṃ ca vāmaṃ brahmasu pañcasu /
madhyaṃ tu liṃgabhāgeṣu yoniṃ ca triṣu hetuṣu // 7.2,35.13 //
prākṛtaṃ ca yathaiśvaryaṃ tasmādviśvaṃ yajurmayam /
tatopasthāpayāmāsa sāmārthaṃ daśadhātmanaḥ // 7.2,35.14 //
tamoguṇeṣvatho rudraṃ mūrtiṣvādyaṃ kriyāsu ca /
saṃhṛtiṃ triṣu lokeṣu tattveṣu śivamuttamam // 7.2,35.15 //
vidyākalāsvaghoraṃ ca tathā brahmasu pañcasu /
liṃgabhāgeṣu pīṭhordhvaṃ bījinaṃ kāraṇatraye // 7.2,35.16 //
pauruṣaṃ ca tathaiśvaryamitthaṃ sāmnā tataṃ jagat /
athātharvāha nairguṇyamarthaṃ prathamamātmanaḥ // 7.2,35.17 //
tato maheśvaraṃ sākṣānmūrtiṣvapi sadāśivam /
kriyāsu niṣkriyasyāpi śivasya paramātmanaḥ // 7.2,35.18 //
bhūtānugrahaṇaṃ caiva mucyaṃte yena jaṃtavaḥ /
lokeṣvapi yato vāco nivṛttā manasā saha // 7.2,35.19 //
tadūrdhvamunmanā lokātsomalokamalaukikam /
somassahomayā yatra nityaṃ nivasatīśvaraḥ // 7.2,35.20 //
tadūrdhvamunmanā lokādyaṃ prāpto na nivartate /
śāṃtiṃ ca śāṃtyatītāṃ ca vyāpikāṃ cai kalāsvapi // 7.2,35.21 //
tatpūruṣaṃ tatheśānaṃ brahma brahmasu pañcasu /
mūrdhānamapi liṃgasya nādabhāgeṣvanuttamam // 7.2,35.22 //
yatrāvāhya samārādhyaḥ kevalo niṣkalaḥ śivaḥ /
tatteṣvapi tadā biṃdornādācchaktestataḥ parāt // 7.2,35.23 //
tattvādapi paraṃ tattvamatattvaṃ paramārthataḥ /
kāraṇeṣu trayātītānmāyāvikṣobhakāraṇāt // 7.2,35.24 //
anaṃtācchuddhavidyāyāḥ parastācca maheśvarāt /
sarvavidyeśvarādhīśānna parācca sadāśivāt // 7.2,35.25 //
sarvamaṃtratanordevācchaktitrayasamanvitāt /
pañcavaktrāddaśabhujātsākṣātsakalaniṣkalāt // 7.2,35.26 //
tasmādapi parādbiṃdorardhedośca tataḥ parāt /
tataḥ parānniśādhīśānnādākhyācca tataḥ parāt // 7.2,35.27 //
tataḥ parātsuṣumneśādbrahmaraṃdhreśvarādapi /
tataḥ parasmācchakteśca parastācchivatattvataḥ // 7.2,35.28 //
paramaṃ kāraṇaṃ sākṣātsvayaṃ niṣkāraṇaṃ śivam /
kāraṇānāṃ ca dhātāraṃ dhyātārāṃ dhyeyamavyayam // 7.2,35.29 //
paramākāśamadhyasthaṃ paramātmopari sthitaṃ /
sarvaiśvaryeṇa saṃpannaṃ sarveśvaramanīśvaram // 7.2,35.30 //
aiśvaryāccāpi māyeyādaśuddhānmānuṣādikāt /
aparācca parāttyājyādadhiśuddhādhvagocarāt // 7.2,35.31 //
tatparācchuddhavidyādyādunmanāṃtātparātparāt /
paramaṃ paramaiśvaryamunmanādyamanādi ca // 7.2,35.32 //
apāramaparādhīnaṃ nirastātiśayaṃ sthiram /
itthamarthairdaśavidhairiyamātharvaṇī śrutiḥ // 7.2,35.33 //
yasmādgarīyasī tasmādviśvaṃ vyāptamatharvaṇāt /
ṛgvedaḥ punarāhedaṃ jāgradrūpaṃ mayocyate // 7.2,35.34 //
yenāhamātmatattvasya nityamasmyabhidhāyakaḥ /
yajurvedo 'vadattadvatsvapnāvasthā mayocyate // 7.2,35.35 //
bhogyātmanā pariṇatā vidyāvedyā yato mayi /
sāma cāha suṣuptyākhyamevaṃ sarvaṃ mayocyate // 7.2,35.36 //
mamārthena śivenedaṃ tāmasenābhidhīyate /
atharvāha turāyākhyaṃ turīyātītameva ca // 7.2,35.37 //
mayābhidhīyate tasmādadhvātītapadosmyaham /
adhvātmakaṃ tu tritayaṃ śivavidyātmasaṃjñitam // 7.2,35.38 //
tattraiguṇyaṃ trayīsādhyaṃ saṃśodhyaṃ ca padaiṣiṇā /
adhvātītaṃ turīyākhyaṃ nirvāṇaṃ paramaṃ padam // 7.2,35.39 //
tadatītaṃ ca nairguṇyādadhvanosya viśodhakam /
dvayoḥ pramāpako nādo nadāṃtaśca madātmakaḥ // 7.2,35.40 //
tasmānmamārthasvātaṃtryātpradhānaḥ parameśvaraḥ /
yadasti vastu tatsarvaṃ guṇapradhānyayogataḥ // 7.2,35.41 //
samastaṃ vyastamapi ca praṇavārthaṃ pracakṣate /
savārthavācakaṃ tasmādekaṃ brahmaitadakṣaram // 7.2,35.42 //
tenomiti jagatkṛtsnaṃ kurute prathamaṃ śivaḥ /
śivo hi praṇavo hyeṣa praṇavo hi śivaḥ smṛtaḥ // 7.2,35.43 //
vācyavācakayorbhedo nātyaṃtaṃ vidyate yataḥ /
ciṃtayā rahito rudro vācoyanmanasā saha // 7.2,35.44 //
aprāpya tannivartaṃte vācyastvekākṣareṇa saḥ /
ekākṣarādakārākhyādātmā brahmābhidhīyate // 7.2,35.45 //
ekākṣarādukārākhyāddvidhā viṣṇurudīryate /
ekākṣarānmakārākhyācchivo rudra udāhṛtaḥ // 7.2,35.46 //
dakṣiṇāṃgānmaheśasya jāto brahmātmasaṃjñikaḥ /
vāmāṃgādabhavadviṣṇustato vidyeti saṃjñitaḥ // 7.2,35.47 //
hṛdayānnīlarudro bhūcchivasya śivasaṃjñikaḥ /
sṛṣṭeḥ pravartako brahmā sthiterviṣṇurvimohakaḥ // 7.2,35.48 //
saṃhārasya tathā rudrastayornityaṃ niyāmakaḥ /
tasmāttrayaste kathyaṃte jagataḥ kāraṇāni ca /
kāraṇatrayahetuśca śivaḥ paramakāraṇam // 7.2,35.50 //
arthametamavijñāya rajasā baddhavairayoḥ /
yuvayoḥ pratibodhāya madhye liṃgamupasthitam // 7.2,35.51 //
evamomiti māṃ prāhuryadihoktamatharvaṇā /
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni śākhāścānyāḥ sahasraśaḥ // 7.2,35.52 //
vedeṣvevaṃ svayaṃ vaktrairvyaktamityavadatsvapi /
svapnānubhūtamiva tattābhyāṃ nādhyavasīyate // 7.2,35.53 //
tayostatra prabodhāya tamopanayanāya ca /
liṃgepi mudritaṃ sarvaṃ yathā vedairudāhṛtam // 7.2,35.54 //
taddṛṣṭvā mudritaṃ liṃge prasādālliṃginastadā /
praśāṃtamanasau devau prabuddhau saṃbabhūvatuḥ // 7.2,35.55 //
utpattiṃ vilayaṃ caiva yathātmyaṃ ca ṣaḍadhvanām /
tataḥ parataraṃ dhāma dhāmavaṃtaṃ ca pūruṣam // 7.2,35.56 //
niruttarataraṃ brahma niṣkalaṃ śivamīśvaram /
paśupāśamayasyāsya prapañcasya sadā patim // 7.2,35.57 //
akutobhayamatyaṃtamavṛddhikṣayamavyayam /
vāhyamābhyaṃtaraṃ vyāptaṃ vāhyābhyaṃtaravarjitam // 7.2,35.58 //
nirastātiśayaṃ śaśvadviśvalokavilakṣaṇam /
alakṣaṇamanirdeśyamavāṅmanasagocaram // 7.2,35.59 //
prakāśaikarasaṃ śāṃtaṃ prasannaṃ satatoditam /
sarvakalyāṇanilayaṃ śaktyā tādṛśayānvitam // 7.2,35.60 //
jñātvā devaṃ virūpākṣaṃ brahmanārāyaṇau tadā /
racayitvāṃjaliṃ mūrdhni bhītau tau vācamūcatuḥ // 7.2,35.61 //
brahmovāca ajño vāhamabhijño vā tvayādau deva nirmitaḥ /
īdṛśīṃ bhrāṃtimāpanna iti ko 'trāparādhyati // 7.2,35.62 //
āstāṃ mamedamajñānaṃ tvayi sannihate prabho /
nirbhayaḥ ko 'bhibhāṣeta kṛtyaṃ svasya parasya vā // 7.2,35.63 //
āvayordevadevasya vivādo 'pi hi śobhanaḥ /
pādapraṇāmaphalado nāthasya bhavato yataḥ // 7.2,35.64 //
viṣṇuruvāca /
stotuṃ deva na vāgasti mahimnaḥ sadṛśī tava /
prabhoragre vidheyānāṃ tūṣṇīṃbhāvo vyatikramaḥ // 7.2,35.65 //
kimatra saṃghaṭetkṛtyamityevāvasarocitam /
ajānannapi yatkiṃcitpralapya tvāṃ nato 'smyaham // 7.2,35.66 //
kāraṇatvaṃ tvayā dattaṃ vismṛtaṃ tava māyayā /
mohito 'haṃkṛtaścāpi punarevāsmi śāsitaḥ // 7.2,35.67 //
vijñāpitaiḥ kiṃ bahubhirbhītosmi bhṛśamīśvara /
yato 'hamaparicchedyaṃ tvāṃ paricchettumudyataḥ // 7.2,35.68 //
tvāmuśaṃti mahādevaṃ bhītānāmārtināśanam /
ato vyatikramaṃ me 'dya kṣaṃtumarhasi śaṃkara // 7.2,35.69 //
iti vijñāpitastābhyām īśvarābhyāṃ maheśvaraḥ /
prīto 'nugṛhya tau devau smitapūrvamabhāṣata // 7.2,35.70 //
īśvara uvāca /
vatsavatsa vidhe viṣṇo māyayā mama mohitau /
yuvāṃ prabhutve 'haṃkṛtya buddhavairo parasparam // 7.2,35.71 //
vivādaṃ yuddhaparyaṃtaṃ kṛtvā noparatau kila /
tataścchinnā prajāsṛṣṭirjagatkāraṇabhūtayoḥ // 7.2,35.72 //
ajñānamānaprabhavādvaimatyādyuvayorapi /
tannivartayituṃ yuṣmaddarpamohau mayaiva tu // 7.2,35.73 //
evaṃ nivāritāvadyaliṃgāvirbhāvalīlayā /
tasmādbhūyo vivādaṃ ca vrīḍāṃ cotsṛjya kṛtsnaśaḥ // 7.2,35.74 //
yathāsvaṃ karma kuryātāṃ bhavaṃtau vītamatsarau /
purā mamājñayā sārdhaṃ samastajñānasaṃhitāḥ // 7.2,35.75 //
yuvābhyāṃ hi mayā dattā kāraṇatvaprasiddhaye /
maṃtraratnaṃ ca sūtrākhyaṃ pañcākṣaramayaṃ param // 7.2,35.76 //
mayopadiṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ tadyuvayoradya vismṛtam /
dadāmi ca punaḥ sarvaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ mamājñayā // 7.2,35.77 //
yato vinā yuvāṃ tena na kṣamau sṛṣṭirakṣaṇe /
evamuktvā mahādevo nārāyaṇapitāmahau // 7.2,35.78 //
maṃtrarājaṃ dadau tābhyāṃ jñānasaṃhitayā saha /
tau labdhvā mahatīṃ divyāmājñāṃ māheśvarīṃ parām // 7.2,35.79 //
mahārthaṃ maṃtraratnaṃ ca tathaiva sakalāḥ kalāḥ /
daṃḍavatpraṇatiṃ kṛtvā devadevasya pādayoḥ // 7.2,35.80 //
atiṣṭhatāṃ vītabhayāvānaṃdāstimitau tadā /
etasminnaṃtare citramiṃdrajālavadaiśvaram // 7.2,35.81 //
liṃgaṃ kvāpi tirobhūtaṃ na tābhyāmupalabhyate /
tato vilapya hāheti sadyaḥpraṇayabhaṃgataḥ // 7.2,35.82 //
kimasatyamidaṃ vṛttamiti coktvā parasparam /
aciṃtyavaibhavaṃ śaṃbhorviciṃtya ca gatavyathau // 7.2,35.83 //
abhyupetya parāṃ maitrīmāliṃgya ca parasparam /
jagadvyāpāramuddiśya jagmaturdevapuṃgavau // 7.2,35.84 //
tataḥ prabhṛti śakrādyāḥ sarva eva surāsurāḥ /
ṛṣayaśca narā nāgā nāryaścāpi vidhānataḥ /
liṃgapratiṣṭhā kurvaṃti liṃge taṃ pūjayaṃti ca // 7.2,35.85 //
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe harividhimohanivāraṇaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca /
bhagavañchrotumicchāmi pratiṣṭhāvidhimuttamam /
liṃgasyāpi ca berasya śivena vihitaṃ yathā // 7.2,36.1 //
upamanyuruvāca /
anātmapratikūle tu divase śuklapakṣake /
śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa kuryālliṃgaṃ pramāṇavat // 7.2,36.2 //
svīkṛtyātha śubhasthānaṃ bhūparīkṣāṃ vidhāya ca /
daśopacārānkurvīta lakṣaṇoddhārapūrvakān // 7.2,36.3 //
teṣāṃ daśopacārāṇāṃ pūrvaṃ pūjya vināyakam /
sthānaśuddhyādikaṃ kṛtvāliṃgaṃ snānālayaṃ nayet // 7.2,36.4 //
śalākayā kāṃcanayā kuṃkumādirasāktayā /
lakṣitaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śilpaśāstreṇa vilikhettataḥ // 7.2,36.5 //
aṣṭamṛtsalilairvātha pañcamṛtsalilaistathā /
liṅgaṃ piṃḍikayā sārdhaṃ pañcagavyaiśca śodhayet // 7.2,36.6 //
savedikaṃ samabhyarcya divyādyaṃ tu jalāśayam /
nītvādhivāsayettatra liṃgaṃ piṃḍikayā saha // 7.2,36.7 //
adhivāsālaye śuddhe sarvaśobhāsamanvite /
satoraṇe sāvaraṇe darbhamālāsamāvṛte // 7.2,36.8 //
diggajāṣṭakasaṃpanne dikpālāṣṭaghaṭānvite /
aṣṭamaṃgalakairyukte kṛtadikpālakārcite // 7.2,36.9 //
tejasaṃ dāravaṃ vāpi kṛtvā padmāsanāṃkitam /
vinyasenmadhyatastatra vipulaṃ pīṭhakālayam // 7.2,36.10 //
dvārapālānsamabhyarcya bhadrādīṃścaturaḥkramāt /
samudraśca vibhadraśca sunaṃdaśca vinaṃdakaḥ // 7.2,36.11 //
snāpayitvā samabhyarcya liṃgaṃ vedikayā saha /
sakūrcābhyāṃ tu vastrābhyāṃ samāveṣṭyaṃ samaṃtataḥ // 7.2,36.12 //
prāpayya śanakaistoyaṃ pīṭhikopari śāyayet /
prākśiraskamadhaḥsūtraṃ piṃḍikāṃ cāsya paścime // 7.2,36.13 //
sarvamaṃgalasaṃyuktaṃ liṃgaṃ tatrādhivāsayet /
pañcarātraṃ trirātraṃ vāpyekarātramathāpi vā // 7.2,36.14 //
visṛjya pūjitaṃ tatra śodhayitvā ca pūrvavat /
saṃpūjyotsavamārgeṇa śayanālayamānayet // 7.2,36.15 //
tatrāpi śayanasthānaṃ kuryānmaṃḍalamadhyataḥ /
śuddhairjalaiḥ snāpayitvā liṃgamabhyarcayetkramāt // 7.2,36.16 //
aiśānyāṃ padmamālikhya śuddhalipte mahītale /
śivakuṃbhaṃ śodhayitvā tatrāvāhya śivaṃ yajet // 7.2,36.17 //
vedīmadhye sitaṃ padmaṃ parikalpya vidhānataḥ /
tasya paścimataścāpi caṃḍikāpadmamālikhet // 7.2,36.18 //
kṣaumādyairvāhatairvastraiḥ puṣpairdarbhairathāpi vā /
prakalpya śayanaṃ tasminhemapuṣpaṃ vinikṣipet // 7.2,36.19 //
tatra liṃgaṃ samānīya sarvamaṃgalaniḥsvanaiḥ /
raktena vastrayugmena sakūrcena samaṃtataḥ // 7.2,36.20 //
saha piṃḍikayāveṣṭya śāyayecca yathā purā /
purastātpadmamālikhya taddaleṣu yathākramam // 7.2,36.21 //
vidyeśakalaśānnyasyenmadhye śaivīṃ ca vardhanīm /
parītya padmatritayaṃ juhuyurdvijasattamāḥ // 7.2,36.22 //
te cāṣṭamūrtayaḥ kalpyāḥ pūrvādiparitaḥ sthitāḥ /
catvāraścātha vā dikṣu svadhyetārassajāpakāḥ // 7.2,36.23 //
juhuyuste viraṃcyādyāścatasro mūrtayaḥ smṛtāḥ /
daiśikaḥ prathamaṃ teṣāmaiśānyāṃ paścime 'tha vā // 7.2,36.24 //
pradhānahomaṃ kurvīta saptadravyairyathākramam /
ācāryātpādamardhaṃ vā juhuyuścāpare dvijāḥ // 7.2,36.25 //
pradhānamekamevātra juhuyādatha vā guruḥ /
pūrvaṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ hutvā ghṛtenāṣṭottaraṃ śatam // 7.2,36.26 //
mūrdhni mūlena liṃgasya śivahastaṃ pravinyaset /
śatamardhaṃ tadardhaṃ vā kramāddravyaiśca saptabhiḥ // 7.2,36.27 //
hutvāhutvā spṛśelliṃgaṃ vedikāṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ /
pūrṇāhutiṃ tato hutvā kramāddadyācca dakṣiṇām // 7.2,36.28 //
ācāryātpādamardhaṃ vā hotḥṇāṃ sthapaterapi /
tadardhaṃ deyamanyebhyaḥ sadasyebhyaśca śaktitaḥ // 7.2,36.29 //
tataḥ śvabhre vṛṣaṃ haimaṃ kūrcaṃ vāpi niveśya ca /
mṛdaṃbhasā pañcagavyaiḥ punaḥ śuddhajalena ca // 7.2,36.30 //
śodhitāṃ caṃdanāliptāṃ śvabhre brahmaśilāṃ kṣipet /
karanyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā navabhiḥ śaktināmabhiḥ // 7.2,36.31 //
haritālādidhātūṃśca bījagaṃdhauṣadhairapi /
śivaśāstroktavidhinā kṣipedbrahmaśilopari // 7.2,36.32 //
pratiliṃgaṃ tu saṃsthāpya kṣīraṃ vṛkṣasamudbhavam /
sthitaṃ buddhvā tadutsṛjya liṃgaṃ brahmaśilopari // 7.2,36.33 //
prāgudakpravarāṃ kiṃcitsthāpayenmūlavidyayā /
piṃḍikāṃ cātha saṃyojya śāktaṃ mūlamanusmaran // 7.2,36.34 //
bandhanaṃ baṃdhakadravyaiḥ kṛtvā sthānaṃ viśodhya ca /
dattvā cārghyaṃ ca puṣpāṇi kuryuryavanikāṃ punaḥ // 7.2,36.35 //
yathāyogyaṃ niṣekādi liṃgasya puratastadā /
ānīya śayanasthānātkalaśānvinyasetkramāt // 7.2,36.36 //
mahāpūjāmathārabhya saṃpūjya kalaśāndaśa /
śivamaṃtramanusmṛtya śivakuṃbhajalāṃtare // 7.2,36.37 //
aṃguṣṭhānāmikāyogādādāya tamudīrayet /
nyasedīśānabhāgasya madhye liṃgasya maṃtravit // 7.2,36.38 //
śaktiṃ nyasettathā vidyāṃ vidyeśāṃśca yathākramam /
liṅgamūle śivajalaistato liṃgaṃ niṣecayet // 7.2,36.39 //
vardhanyāṃ piṃḍikāliṃgaṃ vidyeśakalaśaiḥ punaḥ /
abhiṣicyāsanaṃ paścādādhārādyaṃ prakalpayet // 7.2,36.40 //
kṛtvā pañcakalānyāsaṃ dīptaṃ liṃgamanusmaret /
āvāhayecchivau sākṣātprāñjaliḥ prāgudaṅmukhaḥ // 7.2,36.41 //
vṛṣādhirājamāruhya vimānaṃ vā nabhastalāt /
alaṃkṛtaṃ sahāyāṃtaṃ devyā devamanusmaran /
sarvābharaṇaśobhāḍhyaṃ sarvamaṃgalanisvanaiḥ // 7.2,36.42 //
brahmaviṣṇumaheśārkaśakrādyairdevadānavaiḥ /
ānaṃdaklinnasarvāṃgairvinyastāṃjalimastakaiḥ // 7.2,36.43 //
stuvadbhireva nṛtyadbhirnāmadbhirabhito vṛtam /
tataḥ pañcopacārāṃśca kṛtvā pūjāṃ samāpayet // 7.2,36.44 //
nātaḥ parataraḥ kaścidvidhiḥ pañcopacārakāt /
pratiṣṭhāṃ liṃgavatkuryātpratimāsvapi sarvataḥ // 7.2,36.45 //
lakṣaṇoddhārasamaye kāryaṃ nayanamocanam /
jalādhivāse śayane śāyayettāntvadhomukhīm // 7.2,36.46 //
kumbhodaśāyitāṃ maṃtrairhṛdi tāṃ sanniyojayet /
kṛtālayāṃ parāmāhuḥ pratiṣṭhāmakṛtālayāt // 7.2,36.47 //
śaktaḥ kṛtālayaḥ paścātpratiṣṭhāvidhimācaret /
aśaktaścetpratiṣṭhāpya liṃgaṃ beramathāpi vā // 7.2,36.48 //
śakteranuguṇaṃ paścātprakurvīta śivālayam /
gṛhārcāṃ ca punarvakṣye pratiṣṭhāvidhimuttamam // 7.2,36.49 //
kṛtvā kanīyasaṃberaṃ liṃgaṃ vā lakṣaṇānvitam /
ayane cottare prāpte śuklapakśe śubhe dine // 7.2,36.50 //
devīṃ kṛtvā śubhe deśe tatrābjaṃ pūrvavallikhet /
vikīrya patrapuṣpādyairmadhye kuṃbhaṃ nidhāya ca // 7.2,36.51 //
paritastasya caturaḥ kalaśān dikṣu vinyaset /
pañca brahmāṇi tadbījaisteṣu pañcasu pañcabhiḥ // 7.2,36.52 //
nyasya saṃpūjya mudrādi darśayitvābhirakṣya ca /
viśodhya liṃgaṃ beraṃ vā mṛttoyādyairyathā purā // 7.2,36.53 //
sthāpayetpuṣpasaṃchannamuttarasthe varāsane /
nidhāya puṣpaṃ śirasi prokṣayetprokṣaṇījalaiḥ // 7.2,36.54 //
samabhyarcya punaḥ puṣpairjayaśabdādipūrvakam /
kumbhairīśānavidyāṃtaiḥ snāpayenmūlavidyayā // 7.2,36.55 //
tataḥ pañcakalānyāsaṃ kṛtvā pūjāṃ ca pūrvavat /
nityamārādhayettatra devyā devaṃ trilocanam // 7.2,36.56 //
ekamevātha vā kuṃbhaṃ mūrtimantrasamanvitam /
nyasya padmāṃtare sarvaṃ śeṣaṃ pūrvavadācaret // 7.2,36.57 //
atyaṃtopahataṃ liṃgaṃ viśodhya sthāpayetpunaḥ /
saṃprokṣayedupahatamanāgupahataṃ yajet // 7.2,36.58 //
liṃgāni bāṇasaṃjñāni sthāpanīyāni vā na vā /
tāni pūrvaṃ śivenaiva saṃskṛtāni yatastataḥ // 7.2,36.59 //
śeṣāṇi sthāpanīyāni yāni dṛṣṭāni bāṇavat /
svayamudbhūtaliṃge ca divye cārṣe tathaiva ca // 7.2,36.60 //
apīṭhe pīṭhamāveśya kṛtvā saṃprokṣaṇaṃ vidhim /
yajettatra śivaṃ teṣāṃ pratiṣṭhā na vidhīyate // 7.2,36.61 //
dagdhaṃ ślathaṃ kṣatāṃgaṃ ca kṣipelliṃgaṃ jalāśaye /
saṃdhānayogyaṃ saṃdhāya pratiṣṭhāvidhimācaret // 7.2,36.62 //
berādvā vikalālliṃgāddevapūjāpurassaram /
udvāsya hṛdi saṃdhānaṃ tyāgaṃ vā yuktamācaret // 7.2,36.63 //
ekāhapūjāvihatau kuryāddviguṇamarcanam /
dvirātre ca mahāpūjāṃ saṃprokṣaṇamataḥ param // 7.2,36.64 //
māsādūrdhvamanekāhaṃ pūjā yadi vihanyate /
pratiṣṭhā procyate kaiścitkaiścitsaṃprokṣaṇakramaḥ // 7.2,36.65 //
saṃprokṣaṇe tu liṃgāderdevamudvāsya pūrvavat /
aṣṭapañcakrameṇaiva snāpayitvā mṛdaṃbhasā // 7.2,36.66 //
gavāṃ rasaiśca saṃsnāpya darbhatoyairviśodhya ca /
prokṣayetprokṣaṇītoyairmūlenāṣṭottaraṃ śatam // 7.2,36.67 //
sapuṣpaṃ sakuśaṃ pāṇiṃ nyasya liṃgasya mastake /
pañcavāraṃ japenmūlamaṣṭottaraśataṃ tataḥ // 7.2,36.68 //
tato mūlena mūrdhādipīṭhāṃtaṃ saṃspṛśedapi /
pūjāṃ ca mahatīṃ kuryāddevamāvāhya pūrvavat // 7.2,36.69 //
alabdhe sthāpite liṃge śivasthāne jale 'tha vā /
vahnau ravau tathā vyomni bhagavaṃtaṃ śivaṃ yajet // 7.2,36.70 //
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe ptatiṣṭhāvidhivarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śīkṛṣṇa uvāca /
jñāne kriyāyāṃ caryāyāṃ sāramuddhṛtya saṃgrahāt /
uktaṃ bhagavatā sarvaṃ śrutaṃ śrutisamaṃ mayā // 7.2,37.1 //
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi yogaṃ paramadurlabham /
sādhikāraṃ ca sāṃgaṃ ca savidhiṃ saprayojanam // 7.2,37.2 //
yadyasti maraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ yogādyanupamardataḥ /
sadyaḥ sādhayituṃ śakyaṃ yena syānnātmahā naraḥ // 7.2,37.3 //
tacca tatkāraṇaṃ caiva tatkālakaraṇāni ca /
tadbhedatāratamyaṃ ca vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ // 7.2,37.4 //
upamanyuruvāca /
sthāne pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā kṛṣṇa sarvapraśnārthavedinā /
tataḥ krameṇa tatsarvaṃ vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ // 7.2,37.5 //
niruddhavṛttyaṃtarasyaṃ śive cittasya niścalā /
yā vṛttiḥ sa samāsena yogaḥ sa khalu pañcadhā // 7.2,37.6 //
maṃtrayogaḥsparśayogo bhāvayogastathāparaḥ /
abhāvayogassarvebhyo mahāyogaḥ paro mataḥ // 7.2,37.7 //
maṃtrābhyāsavaśenaiva maṃtravācyārthagocaraḥ /
avyākṣepā manovṛttirmaṃtrayoga udāhṛtaḥ // 7.2,37.8 //
prāṇāyāmamukhā saiva sparśe yogobhidhīyate /
sa maṃtrasparśanirmukto bhāvayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ // 7.2,37.9 //
vilīnāvayavaṃ viśvaṃ rūpaṃ saṃbhāvyate yataḥ /
abhāvayogaḥ saṃprokto 'nābhāsādvastunaḥ sataḥ // 7.2,37.10 //
śivasvabhāva evaikaściṃtyate nirupādhikaḥ /
yathā śaivamanovṛttirmahāyoga ihocyate // 7.2,37.11 //
dṛṣṭe tathānuśravike viraktaṃ viṣaye manaḥ /
yasya tasyādhikārosti yoge nānyasya kasyacit // 7.2,37.12 //
viṣayadvayadoṣāṇāṃ guṇānāmīśvarasya ca /
darśanādeva satataṃ viraktaṃ jāyate manaḥ // 7.2,37.13 //
aṣṭāṃgo vā ṣaḍaṃgo vā sarvayogaḥ samāsataḥ /
yamaśca niyamaścaiva svastikādyaṃ tathāsanam // 7.2,37.14 //
prāṇāyāmaḥ pratyāhāro dhāraṇā dhyānameva ca /
samādhiriti yogāṃgānyaṣṭāvuktāni sūribhiḥ // 7.2,37.15 //
āsanaṃ prāṇasaṃrodhaḥ pratyāhārotha dhāraṇā /
dhyānaṃ samādhiryogasya ṣaḍaṃgāni samāsataḥ // 7.2,37.16 //
pṛthaglakṣaṇameteṣāṃ śivaśāstre samīritam /
śivāgameṣu cānyeṣu viśeṣātkāmikādiṣu // 7.2,37.17 //
yogaśāstreṣvapi tathā purāṇeṣvapi keṣu ca /
ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryāparigrahaḥ /
yama ityucyate sadbhiḥ pañcāvayavayogataḥ // 7.2,37.18 //
śaucaṃ tuṣṭistapaścaiva japaḥ praṇidhireva ca /
iti pañcaprabhedassyānniyamaḥ svāṃśabhedataḥ // 7.2,37.19 //
svastikaṃ padmamadhyeṃduṃ vīraṃ yogaṃ prasādhitam /
paryaṃkaṃ ca yatheṣṭaṃ ca proktamāsanamaṣṭadhā // 7.2,37.20 //
prāṇaḥ svadehajo vāyustasyāyāmo nirodhanam /
tadrocakaṃ pūrakaṃ ca kuṃbhakaṃ ca tridhocyate // 7.2,37.21 //
nāsikāpuṭamaṃgulyā pīḍyaikamapareṇa tu /
audaraṃ recayedvāyuṃ tathāyaṃ recakaḥ smṛtaḥ // 7.2,37.22 //
bāhyena marutā dehaṃ dṛtivatparipūrayet /
nāsāpuṭenāpareṇa pūraṇātpūrakaṃ matam // 7.2,37.23 //
na muṃcati na gṛhṇāti vāyumaṃtarbahiḥ sthitam /
saṃpūrṇaṃ kuṃbhavattiṣṭhedacalaḥ sa tu kuṃbhaka // 7.2,37.24 //
recakādyaṃ trayamidaṃ na drutaṃ na vilaṃbitam /
tadyataḥ kramayogena tvabhyasedyogasādhakaḥ // 7.2,37.25 //
recakādiṣu yobhyāso nāḍīśodhanapūrvakaḥ /
svecchotkramaṇaparyaṃtaḥ prokto yogānuśāsane // 7.2,37.26 //
kanyakādikramavaśātprāṇāyāmanirodhanam /
taccaturdhopadiṣṭaṃ syānmātrāguṇavibhāgataḥ // 7.2,37.27 //
kanyakastu caturdhā syātsa ca dvādaśamātrakaḥ /
madhyamastu dviruddhātaścaturviṃśatimātrakaḥ // 7.2,37.28 //
uttamastu triruddhātaḥ ṣaḍviṃśanmātrakaḥ paraḥ /
svedakaṃpādijanakaḥ prāṇāyāmastaduttaraḥ // 7.2,37.29 //
ānaṃdodbhavaromāṃcanetrāśrūṇāṃ vimocanam /
jalpabhramaṇamūrchādyaṃ jāyate yoginaḥ param // 7.2,37.30 //
jānuṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya na drutaṃ na vilaṃbitam /
aṃgulīsphoṭanaṃ kuryātsā mātreti prakīrtitā // 7.2,37.31 //
mātrākrameṇa vijñeyāścodvātakramayogataḥ /
nāḍīviśuddhipūrvaṃ tu prāṇāyāmaṃ samācaret // 7.2,37.32 //
agarbhaśca sagarbhaśca prāṇāyāmo dvidhā smṛtaḥ /
japaṃ dhyānaṃ vināgarbhaḥ sagarbhastatsamanvayāt // 7.2,37.33 //
agarbhādgarbhasaṃyuktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥśatādhikaḥ /
tasmātsagarbhaṃ kurvanti yoginaḥ prāṇasaṃyamam // 7.2,37.34 //
prāṇasya vijayādeva jīyaṃte deha 1vāyavaḥ /
prāṇo 'pānaḥ samānaśca hyudāno vyāna eva ca // 7.2,37.35 //
nāgaḥ kūrmaśca kṛkalo devadatto dhanaṃjayaḥ /
prayāṇaṃ kurute yasmāttasmātprāṇo 'bhidhīyate // 7.2,37.36 //
avāṅnayatyapānākhyo yadāhārādi bhujyate /
vyāno vyānaśayatyaṃgānyaśeṣāṇi vivardhayan // 7.2,37.37 //
udvejayati marmāṇītyudāno vāyurīritaḥ /
samaṃ nayati sarvāṃgaṃ samānastena gīyate // 7.2,37.38 //
udgāre nāga ākhyātaḥ kūrma unmīlane sthitaḥ /
kṛkalaḥ kṣavathau jñeyo devadatto vijṛṃbhaṇe // 7.2,37.39 //
na jahāti mṛtaṃ cāpi sarvavyāpī dhanaṃjayaḥ /
krameṇābhyasyamānoyaṃ prāṇāyāmapramāṇavān // 7.2,37.40 //
nirdahatyakhilaṃ doṣaṃ karturdehaṃ ca rakṣati /
prāṇe tu vijite samyak taccihnānyupalakṣayet // 7.2,37.41 //
viṇmūtraśleṣmaṇāṃ tāvadalpabhāvaḥ prajāyate /
bahubhojanasāmarthyaṃ cirāducchvāsanaṃ tathā // 7.2,37.42 //
laghutvaṃ śīghragāmitvamutsāhaḥ svarasauṣṭhavam /
sarvarogakṣayaścaiva balaṃ tejaḥ surūpatā // 7.2,37.43 //
dhṛtirmedhā yuvatvaṃ ca sthiratā ca prasannatā /
tapāṃsi pāpakṣayatā yajñadānavratādayaḥ // 7.2,37.44 //
prāṇāyāmasya tasyaite kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm /
indriyāṇi prasaktāni yathāsvaṃ viṣayeṣviha // 7.2,37.45 //
āhatya yannigṛhṇāti sa pratyāhāra ucyate /
namaḥpūrvāṇīṃdriyāṇi svargaṃ narakameva ca // 7.2,37.46 //
nigṛhītanisṛṣṭāni svargāya narakāya ca /
tasmātsukhārthī matimāñjñānavairāgyamāsthitaḥ // 7.2,37.47 //
iṃdriyāśvānnigṛhyāśu svātmanātmānamuddharet /
dhāraṇā nāma cittasya sthānabandhassamāsataḥ // 7.2,37.48 //
sthānaṃ ca śiva evaiko nānyaddoṣatrayaṃ yataḥ /
kālaṃ kaṃcāvadhīkṛtya sthāne 'vasthāpitaṃ manaḥ // 7.2,37.49 //
na tu pracyavate lakṣyāddhāraṇā syānna cānyathā /
manasaḥ prathamaṃ sthairyaṃ dhāraṇātaḥ prajāyate // 7.2,37.50 //
tasmāddhīraṃ manaḥ kuryāddhāraṇābhyāsayogataḥ /
dhyai ciṃtāyāṃ smṛto dhātuḥ śivaciṃtā muhurmuhuḥ // 7.2,37.51 //
avyākṣiptena manasā dhyānaṃ nāma taducyate /
dhyeyāvasthitacittasya sadṛśaḥ pratyayaśca yaḥ // 7.2,37.52 //
pratyayāntaranirmuktaḥ pravāho dhyānamucyate /
sarvamanyatparityajya śiva eva śivaṃkaraḥ // 7.2,37.53 //
paro dhyeyo 'dhideveśaḥ samāptātharvaṇī śrutiḥ /
tathā śivā parā dhyeyā sarvabhūtagatau śivau // 7.2,37.54 //
tau śrutau smṛtiśāstrebhyaḥ sarvagau sarvadoditau /
sarvajñau satataṃ dhyeyau nānārūpavibhedataḥ // 7.2,37.55 //
vimuktiḥ pratyayaḥ pūrvaḥ pratyayaścāṇimādikam /
ityetaddvividhaṃ jñeyaṃ dhyānasyāsya prayojanam // 7.2,37.56 //
dhyātā dhyānaṃ tathā dhyeyaṃ yacca dhyānaprayojanam /
etaccatuṣṭayaṃ jñātvā yogaṃ yuñjīta yogavit // 7.2,37.57 //
jñānavairāgyasaṃpannaḥ śraddadhānaḥ kṣamānvitaḥ /
nirmamaśca sadotsāhī dhyātetthaṃ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ // 7.2,37.58 //
japācchrāṃtaḥ punardhyāyeddhyānācchrāṃtaḥ punarjapet /
japadhyanābhiyuktasya kṣipraṃ yogaḥ prasiddhyati // 7.2,37.59 //
dhāraṇā dvādaśāyāmā dhyānaṃ dvādaśadhāraṇam /
dhyānadvādaśakaṃ yāvatsamādhirabhidhīyate // 7.2,37.60 //
samādhirnnāma yogāṃgamantimaṃ parikīrtitam /
samādhinā ca sarvatra prajñālokaḥ pravartate // 7.2,37.61 //
yadarthamātranirbhāsaṃ stimito dadhivatsthitam /
svarūpaśūnyavadbhānaṃ samādhirabhidhīyate // 7.2,37.62 //
dhyeye manaḥ samāveśya paśyedapi ca susthiram /
nirvāṇānalavadyogī samādhisthaḥ pragīyate // 7.2,37.63 //
na śṛṇoti na cāghrāti na jalpati na paśyati /
na ca sparśaṃ vijānāti na saṃkalpayate manaḥ // 7.2,37.64 //
navābhimanyate kiṃcidbadhyate na ca kāṣṭavat /
evaṃ śive vilīnātmā samādhistha ihocyate // 7.2,37.65 //
yathā dīpo nivātasthaḥ spandate na kadācana /
tathā samādhiniṣṭho 'pi tasmānna vicaletsudhīḥ // 7.2,37.66 //
evamabhyasataścāraṃ yogino yogamuttamam /
tadantarāyā naśyaṃti vighnāḥ sarve śanaiḥśanaiḥ // 7.2,37.67 //
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ vāyunaimiṣeyarṣisaṃvāde uttarakhaṇḍe yogagativarṇanaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
upamanyuruvāca /
ālasyaṃ vyādhayastīvrāḥ pramādaḥ sthānasaṃśayaḥ /
anavasthitacittatvamaśraddhā bhrāṃtidarśanam // 7.2,38.1 //
duḥkhāni daurmanasyaṃ ca viṣayeṣu ca lolatā /
daśaite yuñjatāṃ puṃsāmantarāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ // 7.2,38.2 //
ālasyamalasattvaṃ tu yogināṃ dehacetanoḥ /
dhātuvaiṣamyajā doṣā vyādhayaḥ karmadoṣajāḥ // 7.2,38.3 //
pramādo nāma yogasya sādhanā nāma bhāvanā /
idaṃ vetyubhayākrāntaṃ vijñānaṃ sthānasaṃśayaḥ // 7.2,38.4 //
apratiṣṭhā hi manasastvanavasthitirucyate /
aśraddhā bhāvarahitā vṛttirvai yogavartmani // 7.2,38.5 //
viparyastā matiryā sā bhrāṃtirityabhidhīyate /
duḥkhamajñānajaṃ puṃsāṃ cittasyādhyātmikaṃ viduḥ // 7.2,38.6 //
ādhibhautikamaṃgotthaṃ yacca duḥkhaṃ purā kṛtaiḥ /
ādhidaivikamākhyātamaśanyastraviṣādikam // 7.2,38.7 //
icchāvighātajaṃ mokṣaṃ daurmanasyaṃ pracakṣate /
viṣayeṣu vicitreṣu vibhramastatra lolatā // 7.2,38.8 //
śānteṣveteṣu vighneṣu yogāsaktasya yoginaḥ /
upasargāḥ pravartaṃte divyāste siddhisūcakāḥ // 7.2,38.9 //
pratibhā śravaṇaṃ vārtā darśanāsvādavedanāḥ /
upasargāḥ ṣaḍityete vyaye yogasya siddhayaḥ // 7.2,38.10 //
sūkṣme vyavahite 'tīte viprakṛṣṭe tvanāgate /
pratibhā kathyate yo 'rthe pratibhāso yathātatham // 7.2,38.11 //
śravaṇaṃ sarvaśabdānāṃ śravaṇe cāprayatnataḥ /
vārttā vārttāsu vijñānaṃ sarveṣāmeva dehinām // 7.2,38.12 //
darśanaṃ nāma divyānāṃ darśanaṃ cāprayatnataḥ /
tathāsvādaśca divyeṣu raseṣvāsvāda ucyate // 7.2,38.13 //
sparśanādhigamastadvadvedanā nāma viśrutā /
gandhādīnāṃ ca divyānāmābrahmabhuvanādhipāḥ // 7.2,38.14 //
saṃtiṣṭhante ca ratnāni prayacchaṃti bahūni ca /
svacchandamadhurā vāṇī vividhāsyātpravartate // 7.2,38.15 //
rasāyanāni sarvāṇi divyāścauṣadhayastathā /
sidhyaṃti praṇipatyainaṃ diśaṃti surayoṣitaḥ // 7.2,38.16 //
yogasiddhyaikadeśe 'pi dṛṣṭe mokṣe bhavenmatiḥ /
dṛṣṭametanmayā yadvattadvanmokṣo bhavediti // 7.2,38.17 //
kṛśatā sthūlatā bālyaṃ vārdhakyaṃ caiva yauvanam /
nānācātisvarūpaṃ ca caturṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam // 7.2,38.18 //
pārthivāṃśaṃ vinā nityaṃ surabhirgandhasaṃgrahaḥ /
evamaṣṭaguṇaṃ prāhuḥ paiśācaṃ pārthivaṃ padam // 7.2,38.19 //
jale nivasanaṃ caiva bhūmyāmevaṃ vinirgamaḥ /
icchecchaktaḥ svayaṃ pātuṃ samudramapi nāturaḥ // 7.2,38.20 //
yatrecchati jagatyasmiṃstatraiva jaladarśanam /
vinā kumbhādikaṃ pāṇau jalasañcayadhāraṇam // 7.2,38.21 //
yadvastu virasañcāpi bhoktumicchati tatkṣaṇāt /
rasādikaṃ bhaveccānyattrayāṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam // 7.2,38.22 //
nirvraṇatvaṃ śarīrasya pārthivaiśca samanvitam /
tadidaṃ ṣoḍaśaguṇamāpyamaiśvaryamadbhutam // 7.2,38.23 //
śarīrādagninirmāṇaṃ tattāpabhayavarjanam /
śaktirjagadidaṃ dagdhuṃ yadīcchedaprayatnataḥ // 7.2,38.24 //
sthāpanaṃ vānalasyā 'psu pāṇau pāvakadhāraṇam /
dagdhe sarge yathāpūrvaṃ mukhe cānnādipācanam /
dvābhyāṃ dehavinirmāṇamāpyaiśvaryasamanvitam // 7.2,38.25 //
etaccaturviṃśatidhā taijasaṃ paricakṣate /
manojavatvaṃ bhūtānāṃ kṣaṇādantaḥpraveśanam // 7.2,38.26 //
parvatādimahābhāradhāraṇañcāprayatnataḥ /
gurutvañca laghutvañca pāṇāvaniladhāraṇam // 7.2,38.27 //
aṃgulyagranipātādyairbhūmerapi ca kampanam /
ekena dehaniṣpattiryuktaṃ bhogaiśca taijasaiḥ // 7.2,38.28 //
dvātriṃśadguṇamaiśvaryaṃ mārutaṃ kavayo viduḥ /
chāyāhīnaviniṣpattirindriyāṇāmadarśanam // 7.2,38.29 //
khecaratvaṃ yathākāmamindriyārthasamanvayaḥ /
ākāśalaṃghanaṃ caiva svadehe tanniveśanam // 7.2,38.30 //
ākāśapiṇḍīkaraṇamaśarīratvameva ca /
anilaiśvaryasaṃyuktaṃ catvāriṃśadguṇaṃ mahat // 7.2,38.31 //
aindramaiśvaryamākhyātamāmbaraṃ tatpracakṣate /
yathākāmopalabdhiśca yathākāmavinirgamaḥ // 7.2,38.32 //
sarvasyābhibhavaścaiva sarvaguhyārthadarśanam /
karmānurūpanirmāṇaṃ vaśitvaṃ priyadarśanam // 7.2,38.33 //
saṃsāradarśanaṃ caiva bhogairaindraissamanvitam /
etaccāṃdramasaiśvaryaṃ mānasaṃ guṇato 'dhikam // 7.2,38.34 //
chedanaṃ tāḍanaṃ caiva baṃdhanaṃ mocanaṃ tathā /
grahaṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃsāravaśavartinām // 7.2,38.35 //
prasādaścāpi sarveṣāṃ mṛtyukālajayastathā /
ābhimānikamaiśvaryaṃ prājāpatyaṃ pracakṣate // 7.2,38.36 //
etaccāndramasairbhogaiḥ ṣaṭpañcāśadguṇaṃ mahat /
sargaḥ saṃkalpamātreṇa trāṇaṃ saṃharaṇaṃ tathā // 7.2,38.37 //
svādhikāraśca sarveṣāṃ bhūtacittapravartanam /
asādṛśyaṃ ca sarvasya nirmāṇaṃ jagataḥ pṛthak // 7.2,38.38 //
śubhāśubhasya karaṇaṃ prājāpatyaiśca saṃyutam /
catuṣṣaṣṭhiguṇaṃ brāhmamaiśvaryaṃ ca pracakṣate // 7.2,38.39 //
bauddhādasmātparaṃ gauṇamaiśvaryaṃ prākṛtaṃ viduḥ /
vaiṣṇavaṃ tatsamākhyātaṃ tasyaiva bhuvanasthitiḥ /
brahmaṇā tatpadaṃ sarvaṃ vaktumanyairna śakyate // 7.2,38.40 //
tatpauruṣaṃ ca gauṇaṃ ca gaṇeśaṃ padamaiśvaram /
viṣṇunā tatpadaṃ kiṃcijjñātumanyairna śakyate // 7.2,38.41 //
vijñānasiddhayaścaiva sarvā evaupasargikāḥ /
niroddhavyā prayatnena varrāgyeṇa pareṇa tu // 7.2,38.42 //
pratibhāseṣvaśuddheṣu guṇeṣvāsaktacetasaḥ /
na sidhyetparamaiśvaryamabhayaṃ sārvakāmikam // 7.2,38.43 //
tasmādguṇāṃśca bhogāṃśca devāsuramahībhṛtām /
tṛṇavadyastyajettasya yogasiddhiḥ parā bhavet // 7.2,38.44 //
athavānugrahecchāyāṃ jagato vicarenmuniḥ /
yathākāmaṃguṇānbhogānbhuktvā muktiṃ prayāsyati // 7.2,38.45 //
atha prayogaṃ yogasya vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ /
śubhe kāle śubhe deśe śivakṣetrādike punaḥ /
vijane jaṃturahite niḥśabde bādhavarjite // 7.2,38.46 //
supralipte sthale saumye gandhadhūpādivāsite /
muktapuṣpasamākīrṇe vitānādi vicitrite // 7.2,38.47 //
kuśapuṣpasamittoyaphalamūlasamanvite /
nāgnyabhyāśe jalābhyāśe śuṣkaparṇacaye 'pi vā // 7.2,38.48 //
na daṃśamaśakākīrṇe sarpaśvāpadasaṃkule /
na ca duṣṭamṛgākīrṇe na bhaye durjanāvṛte // 7.2,38.49 //
śmaśāne caityavalmīke jīrṇāgāre catuṣpathe /
nadīnadasamudrāṇāṃ tīre rathyāṃtare 'pi vā // 7.2,38.50 //
na jīrṇodyānagoṣṭhādau nāniṣṭe na ca niṃdite /
nājīrṇāmlarasodgāre na ca viṇmūtradūṣite // 7.2,38.51 //
nacchardyāmātisāre vā nātibhuktau śramānvite /
na cāticiṃtākulito na cātikṣutpipāsitaḥ // 7.2,38.52 //
nāpi svagurukarmādau prasakto yogamācaret /
yuktāhāravihāraśca yuktaceṣṭaśca karmasu // 7.2,38.53 //
yuktanidrāprabodhaśca sarvāyāsavivarjitaḥ /
āsanaṃ mṛdulaṃ ramyaṃ vipulaṃ susamaṃ śuci // 7.2,38.54 //
padmakasvastikādīnāmabhyasedāsaneṣu ca /
abhivaṃdya svagurvaṃtānabhivādyānanukramāt // 7.2,38.55 //
ṛjugrīvaśirovakṣā nātiṣṭhecchiṣṭalocanaḥ /
kiṃcidunnāmitaśirā daṃtairdaṃtānna saṃspṛśet // 7.2,38.56 //
daṃtāgrasaṃsthitā jihvāmacalāṃ sanniveśya ca /
pārṣṇibhyāṃ vṛṣaṇau rakṣaṃstathā prajananaṃ punaḥ // 7.2,38.57 //
ūrvorupari saṃsthāpya bāhū tiryagayatnataḥ /
dakṣiṇaṃ karapṛṣṭhaṃ tu nyasya vāmatalopari // 7.2,38.58 //
unnāmya śanakaiḥ pṛṣṭhamuro viṣṭabhya cāgrataḥ /
saṃprekṣya nāsikāgraṃ svaṃ diśaścānavalokayan // 7.2,38.59 //
saṃbhṛtaprāṇasaṃcāraḥ pāṣāṇa iva niścalaḥ /
svadehāyatanasyāṃtarviciṃtya śivamaṃbayā // 7.2,38.60 //
hṛtpadmapīṭhikāmadhye dhyānayajñena pūjayet /
mūle nāsāgrato nābhau kaṃṭhe vā tāluraṃdhrayoḥ // 7.2,38.61 //
bhrūmadhye dvāradeśe vā lalāṭe mūrdhni vā smaret /
parikalpya yathānyāyaṃ śivayoḥ paramāsanam // 7.2,38.62 //
tatra sāvaraṇaṃ vāpi nirāvaraṇameva vā /
dvidaleṣoḍaśāre vā dvādaśāre yathāvidhi // 7.2,38.63 //
daśāre vā ṣaḍasre vā caturasre śivaṃ smaret /
bhruvoraṃtarataḥ padmaṃ dvidalaṃ taḍidujjvalam // 7.2,38.64 //
bhrūmadhyasthāravindasya kramādvai dakṣiṇottare /
vidyutsamānavarṇe ca parṇe varṇāvasānake // 7.2,38.65 //
ṣoḍaśārasya patrāṇi svarāḥ ṣoḍaśa tāni vai /
pūrvādīni kramādetatpadmaṃ kandasya mūlataḥ // 7.2,38.66 //
kakārādiṭakārāṃtā varṇāḥ parṇānyanukramāt /
bhānuvarṇasya padmasya dhyeyaṃ tad 1dhṛdayāntare // 7.2,38.67 //
gokṣīradhavalasyoktā ḍādiphāntā yathākramam /
adho dalasyāmbujasya etasya ca dalāni ṣaṭ // 7.2,38.68 //
vidhūmāṃgāravarṇasya varṇā vādyāśca lāntimāḥ /
mūlādhārāraviṃdasya hemābhasya yathākramam /
vakārādisakārāntā varṇāḥ parṇamayāḥ sthitāḥ // 7.2,38.69 //
eteṣvathāraviṃdeṣu yatraivābhirataṃ manaḥ /
tatraiva devaṃ devīṃ ca ciṃtayeddhīrayā dhiyā // 7.2,38.70 //
aṃguṣṭhamātramamalaṃ dīpyamānaṃ samaṃtataḥ /
śuddhadīpaśikhākāraṃ svaśaktyā pūrṇamaṇḍitam // 7.2,38.71 //
indurekhāsamākāraṃ tārārūpamathāpi vā /
nīvāraśūkassadṛśaṃ bisasutrābhameva vā // 7.2,38.72 //
kadambagolakākāraṃ tuṣārakaṇikopamam /
kṣityāditattvavijayaṃ dhyātā yadyapi vāñchati // 7.2,38.73 //
tattattattvādhipāmeva mūrtiṃ sthūlāṃ viciṃtayet /
sadāśivāṃtā brahmādyabhavādyāścāṣṭamūrtayaḥ // 7.2,38.74 //
śivasya mūrtayaḥ sthūlāḥ śivaśāstre viniścitāḥ /
ghorā miśrā praśāntāśca mūrtayastā munīśvaraiḥ // 7.2,38.75 //
phalābhilāṣarahitaiścintyāścintāviśāradaiḥ /
ghorāścecciṃtitāḥ kuryuḥ pāparogaparikṣayam // 7.2,38.76 //
cireṇa miśre saumye tu na sadyo na cirādapi /
saumye muktirviśeṣeṇa śāṃtiḥ prajñā prasidhyati // 7.2,38.77 //
sidhyaṃti siddhayaścātra kramaśo nātra saṃśayaḥ /
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe yogagatau vighnotpattivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
upamanyuruvāca /
śrīkaṃṭhanāthaṃ smaratāṃ sadyaḥ sarvārthasiddhayaḥ /
prasidhyaṃtīti matvaike taṃ vai dhyāyaṃti yoginaḥ // 7.2,39.1 //
sthityarthaṃ manasaḥ kecitsthūladhyānaṃ prakurvate /
sthūlaṃ tu niścalaṃ ceto bhavetsūkṣme tu tatsthiram // 7.2,39.2 //
śive tu ciṃtite sākṣātsarvāḥ sidhyanti siddhayaḥ /
mūrtyaṃtareṣu dhyāteṣu śivarūpaṃ viciṃtayet // 7.2,39.3 //
lakṣayenmanasaḥ sthairyaṃ tattaddhyāyetpunaḥ punaḥ /
dhyānamādau saviṣayaṃ tato nirviṣayaṃ jaguḥ // 7.2,39.4 //
tatra nirviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ nāstītyeva satāṃ matam /
buddherhi santatiḥ kāciddhyānamityabhidhīyate // 7.2,39.5 //
tena nirviṣayā buddhiḥ kevaleha pravartate /
tasmātsaviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ bālārkakiraṇāśrayam // 7.2,39.6 //
sūkṣmāśrayaṃ nirviṣayaṃ nāparaṃ paramārthataḥ /
yadvā saviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ tatsākārasamāśrayam // 7.2,39.7 //
nirākārātmasaṃvittirdhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ matam /
nirbījaṃ ca sabījaṃ ca tadeva dhyānamucyate // 7.2,39.8 //
nirākāraśrayatvena sākārāśrayatastathā /
tasmātsaviṣayaṃ dhyānamādau kṛtvā sabījakam // 7.2,39.9 //
aṃte nirviṣayaṃ kuryānnirbījaṃ sarvasiddhaye /
prāṇāyāmena sidhyaṃti devyāḥ śāṃtyādayaḥ kramāt // 7.2,39.10 //
śāṃtiḥ praśāṃtirdīptiśca prasādaśca tataḥ param /
śamaḥ sarvāpadāṃ caiva śāṃtirityabhidhīyate // 7.2,39.11 //
tamaso 'ntabahirnāśaḥ praśāntiḥ parigīyate /
bahirantaḥprakāśo yo dīptirityabhidhīyate // 7.2,39.12 //
svasthatā yā tu sā buddhaḥ prasādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ /
kāraṇāni ca sarvāṇi sabāhyābhyaṃtarāṇi ca // 7.2,39.13 //
buddheḥ prasādataḥ kṣipraṃ prasannāni bhavantyuta /
dhyātā dhyānaṃ tathā dhyeyaṃ yadvā dhyānaprayojanam /
etaccatuṣṭayaṃ jñātvā dhyātā dhyānaṃ samācaret // 7.2,39.14 //
jñānavairāgyasaṃpanno nityamavyagramānasaḥ /
śraddadhānaḥ prasannātmā dhyātā sadbhirudāhṛtaḥ // 7.2,39.15 //
dhyai ciṃtāyāṃ smṛto dhātuḥ śivaciṃtā muhurmuhuḥ /
yogābhyāsastathālpe 'pi yathā pāpaṃ vināśayet /
dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇamātraṃ vā śraddhayā parameśvaram // 7.2,39.17 //
avyākṣiptena manasā dhyānamityabhidhīyate /
buddhipravāharūpasya dhyānasyāsyāvalaṃbanam /
dhyeyamityucyate sadbhistacca sāṃbaḥ svayaṃ śivaḥ // 7.2,39.19 //
vimuktipratyayaṃ pūrṇamaiśvaryaṃ cāṇimādikam /
śivadhyānasya pūrṇasya sākṣāduktaṃ prayojanam // 7.2,39.20 //
yasmātsaukhyaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca dhyānādabhayamāpnuyāt /
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya dhyānayukto bhavennaraḥ // 7.2,39.21 //
nāsti dhyānaṃ vinā jñānaṃ nāsti dhyānamayoginaḥ /
dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ ca yasyāsti tīrṇastena bhavārṇavaḥ // 7.2,39.22 //
jñānaṃ prasannamekāgramaśeṣopādhivarjitam /
yogābhyāsena yuktasya yoginastveva sidhyati // 7.2,39.23 //
prakṣīṇāśeṣapāpānāṃ jñāne dhyāne bhavenmatiḥ /
pāpopahatabuddhīnāṃ tadvārtāpi sudurlabhā // 7.2,39.24 //
yathāvahnirmahādīptaḥ śuṣkamārdraṃ ca nirdahet /
tathā śubhāśubhaṃ karma dhyānāgnirdahate kṣaṇāt // 7.2,39.25 //
atyalpo 'pi yathā dīpaḥ sumahannāśayettamaḥ /
yogābhyāsastathālpo 'pi mahāpāpaṃ vināśayet // 7.2,39.26 //
dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇamātraṃ vā śraddhayā parameśvaram /
yadbhavetsumahacchreyastasyāṃto naiva vidyate // 7.2,39.27 //
nāsti dhyānasamaṃ tīrthaṃ nāsti dhyānasamaṃ tapaḥ /
nāsti dhyānasamo yajñastasmāddhyānaṃ samācaret // 7.2,39.28 //
tīrthāni toyapūrṇāni devānpāṣāṇamṛnmayān /
yogino na prapadyaṃte svātmapratyayakāraṇāt // 7.2,39.29 //
yogināṃ ca vapuḥ sūkṣmaṃ bhavetpratyakṣamaiśvaram /
yathā sthūlamayuktānāṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyaiḥ prakalpitam // 7.2,39.30 //
yathehāṃtaścarā rājñaḥ priyāḥ syurna bahiścarāḥ /
tathāṃtardhyānaniratāḥ priyāśśaṃbhorna karmiṇaḥ // 7.2,39.31 //
bahiskarā yathā loke nātīva phalabhoginaḥ /
dṛṣṭvā narendrabhavane tadvadatrāpi karmiṇaḥ // 7.2,39.32 //
yadyaṃtarā vipadyaṃte jñānayogārthamudyataḥ /
yogasyodyogamātreṇa rudralokaṃ gamiṣyati // 7.2,39.33 //
anubhūya sukhaṃ tatra sa jāto yogināṃ kule /
jñānayogaṃ punarlabdhvā saṃsāramativartate // 7.2,39.34 //
jijñāsurapi yogasya yāṃ gatiṃ labhate naraḥ /
na tāṃ gatimavāpnoti sarvairapi mahāmakhaiḥ // 7.2,39.35 //
dvijānāṃ vedaviduṣāṃ koṭiṃ saṃpūjya yatphalam /
bhikṣāmātrapradānena tatphalaṃ śivayogine // 7.2,39.36 //
yajñāgnihotradānena tīrthahomeṣu yatphalam /
yogināmannadānena tatsamastaṃ phalaṃ labhet // 7.2,39.37 //
ye cāpavādaṃ kurvaṃti vimūḍhāśśivayoginām /
śrotṛbhiste prapadyante narakeṣvāmahīkṣayāt // 7.2,39.38 //
sati śrotari vaktāsyādapavādasya yoginām /
tasmācchrotā ca pāpīyāndaṇḍyassumahatāṃ mataḥ /
ye punaḥ satataṃ bhaktyā bhajaṃti śavayoginaḥ // 7.2,39.39 //
te vidaṃti mahābhogānaṃte yogaṃ ca śāṃkaram /
bhogārthibhirnaraistasmātsaṃpūjyāḥ śivayoginaḥ // 7.2,39.40 //
pratiśrayānnapānādyaiḥ śayyāprāvaraṇādibhiḥ /
yogadharmaḥ sasāratvādabhedyaḥ pāpamudgaraiḥ // 7.2,39.41 //
vajrataṃdulavajjñeyaṃ tathā pāpena yoginaḥ /
na lipyaṃte ca tāpaughaiḥ padmapatraṃ yathāṃbhasā // 7.2,39.42 //
yasmindeśe vasennityaṃ śivayogarato muniḥ /
so 'pi deśo bhavetpūtaḥ sapūta iti kiṃ punaḥ // 7.2,39.43 //
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya kṛtyamanyadvicakṣaṇaḥ /
sarvaduḥkhaprahāṇāya śivayogaṃ samabhyaset // 7.2,39.44 //
siddhayogaphalo yogī lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā /
bhogānbhuktvā yathākāmaṃ viharedvātra vartatām // 7.2,39.45 //
athavā kṣudramityeva matvā vaiṣayikaṃ sukham /
tyaktvā virāgayogena svecchayā karma mucyatām // 7.2,39.46 //
yastvāsannāṃ mṛtiṃ martyo dṛṣṭāriṣṭaṃ ca bhūyasā /
sa yogārambhanirataḥ śivakṣetraṃ samāśrayet // 7.2,39.47 //
sa tatra nivasanneva yadi dhīramanā naraḥ /
prāṇānvināpi rogādyaiḥ svayameva parityajet // 7.2,39.48 //
kṛtvāpyanaśanaṃ caiva hutvā cāṃgaṃ śivānale /
kṣiptvā vā śivatīrtheṣu svadehamavagāhanāt // 7.2,39.49 //
śivaśāstroktavidhivatprāṇānyastu parityajet /
sadya eva vimucyeta nātra kāryā vicāraṇā // 7.2,39.50 //
rogādyairvātha vivaśaḥ śivakṣetraṃ samāśritaḥ /
mriyate yadi sopyevaṃ mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ // 7.2,39.51 //
yathā hi maraṇaṃ śreṣṭhamuśaṃtyanaśanādibhiḥ /
śāstraviśraṃbhadhīreṇa manasā kriyate yataḥ // 7.2,39.52 //
śivanindārataṃ hatvā pīḍitaḥ svayameva vā /
yastyajeddustyajānprāṇānna sa bhūyaḥ prajāyate // 7.2,39.53 //
śivanindārataṃ haṃtumaśakto yaḥ svayaṃ mṛtaḥ /
sadya eva pramucyeta triḥ saptakulasaṃyutaḥ // 7.2,39.54 //
śivārthe yastyajetprāṇāñchivabhaktārthameva vā /
na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścinmuktimārgasthito naraḥ // 7.2,39.55 //
tasmācchīghratarā muktistasya saṃsāramaṃḍalāt /
eteṣvanyatamopāyaṃ kathamapyavalambya vā // 7.2,39.56 //
ṣaḍadhvaśuddhiṃ vidhivatprāpto vā mriyate yadi /
paśūnāmiva tasyeha na kuryādaurdhvadaihikam // 7.2,39.57 //
naivāśaucaṃ prapadyeta tatputrādiviśeṣataḥ /
śivacārārthamathavā śivavidyārthameva vā /
khanedvā bhuvi taddehaṃ dahedvā śucināgninā // 7.2,39.58 //
kṣipedvāpsu śivāsveva tyajedvā kāṣṭhaloṣṭavat /
athainamapi coddiśya karma cetkartumīpsitam // 7.2,39.59 //
kalyāṇameva kurvīta śaktyā bhaktāṃśca tarpayet /
dhanaṃ tasya bhajecchaivaḥ śaivī cetasya santatiḥ // 7.2,39.60 //
nāsti cettacchive dadyānnadadyātpaśusantatiḥ // śivp_7.2,39. 60ef/
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śaivayogavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīsūta uvāca /
iti sa vijitamanyoryādavenopamanyoradhigatamabhidhāya jñānayogaṃ munibhyaḥ /
praṇatimupagatebhyastebhya udbhāvitātmā sapadi viyati vāyuḥ sāyamantarhito 'bhūt // 7.2,40.1 //
tataḥ prabhātasamaye naimiṣīyāstapodhanāḥ /
satrānte 'vabhṛthaṃ kartuṃ sarva eva samudyayuḥ // 7.2,40.2 //
tadā brahmasamādeśāddevī sākṣātsarasvatī /
prasannā svādusalilā prāvartata nadīśubhā // 7.2,40.3 //
sarasvatīṃ nadīṃ dṛṣṭvā munayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ /
samāpya satraṃ prārabdhaṃ cakrustatrāvagāhanam // 7.2,40.4 //
atha saṃtarpya devādīṃstadīyaiḥ salilaiḥ śivaiḥ /
smarantaḥ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ yayurvārāṇasīṃ prati // 7.2,40.5 //
tadā te himavatpādātpaṃtatīṃ dakṣiṇāmukhīm /
dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathī tatra snātvā tattīrato yayuḥ // 7.2,40.6 //
tato vārāṇasīṃ prāpya muditāssarva eva te /
tadottarapravāhāyāṃ gaṃgāyāmavagāhya ca // 7.2,40.7 //
avimukteśvaraṃ liṃgaṃ dṛṣṭvābhyarcya vidhānataḥ /
prayātumudyatāstatra dadṛśurdivi bhāsvaram // 7.2,40.8 //
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ tejodivyaṃ mahādbhutam /
ātmaprabhāvitānena vyāptasarvadigantaram // 7.2,40.9 //
atha pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasmasañchannavigrahāḥ /
munayo 'bhyetya śataśo līnāḥ syustatra tejasi // 7.2,40.10 //
tathā vilīyamāneṣu tapasviṣu mahātmasu /
sadyastirodadhe tejastadadbhutamivābhavat // 7.2,40.11 //
taddṛṣṭvā mahadāścaryaṃ naimiṣīyā maharṣayaḥ /
kimetadityajānanto yayurbrahmavanaṃ prati // 7.2,40.12 //
prāgevaiṣāṃ tu gamanātpavano lokapāvanaḥ /
darśanaṃ naimiṣīyāṇāṃ saṃvādastairmahātmanaḥ // 7.2,40.13 //
śaddhāṃ buddhiṃ tatasteṣāṃ sāṃbe sānucare śive /
samāptiṃ cāpi satrasya dīrghapūrvasya satriṇām // 7.2,40.14 //
vijñāpya jagatāṃ dhātre brahmaṇe brahmayonaye /
svakārye tadanujñāto jagāma svapuraṃ prati // 7.2,40.15 //
atha sthānagato brahmā tumburornāradasya ca /
paraspara spardhitayorgāne vivadamānayoḥ // 7.2,40.16 //
tadudbhāvitagānottharasairmādhyasthamācaran /
gandharvairapsarobhiśca sukhamāste niṣevitaḥ // 7.2,40.17 //
tadānavasarādeva dvāḥsthairdvāri nivāritāḥ /
munayo brahmabhavanādbahiḥ pārśvamupāviśan // 7.2,40.18 //
atha tumburuṇā gāne samatāṃ prāpya nāradaḥ /
sāhacaryeṣvanujñāto brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā // 7.2,40.19 //
tyaktvā parasparaspardhāṃ maitrīṃ ca paramāṃ gataḥ /
saha tenāpsarobhiśca gandharvaiśca samāvṛtaḥ // 7.2,40.20 //
upavīṇayituṃ devaṃ nakulīśvaramīśvaram /
bhavanānniryayau dhāturjaladādaṃśumāniva // 7.2,40.21 //
taṃ dṛṣṭvā ṣaṭkulīyāste nāradaṃ munigovṛṣam /
praṇamyāvasaraṃ śaṃbhoḥ papracchuḥ paramādarāt // 7.2,40.22 //
sa cāvasara evāyamitoṃtargamyatāmiti /
vadanyayāvanyaparastvarayā parayā yutaḥ // 7.2,40.23 //
tato dvāri sthitā ye vai brahmaṇe tānnyavedayan /
tena te viviśurveśma piṃḍībhūyāṃḍajanmanaḥ // 7.2,40.24 //
praviśya dūrato devaṃ praṇamya bhuvi daṃḍavat /
samīpe tadanujñātāḥ parivṛtyopatasthire // 7.2,40.25 //
tāṃstatrāvasthitān pṛṣṭvā kuśalaṃ kamalāsanaḥ /
vṛttāṃtaṃ vo mayā jñātaṃ vāyurevāha no yataḥ // 7.2,40.26 //
bhavadbhiḥ kiṃ kṛtaṃ paścānmāruteṃtarhite sati /
ityuktavati deveśe munayo 'vabhṛthātparam // 7.2,40.27 //
gaṃgātīrthesya gamanaṃ yātrāṃ vārāṇasīṃ prati /
darśanaṃ tatra liṃgānāṃ sthāpitānāṃ sureśvaraiḥ // 7.2,40.28 //
avimukteśvarasyāpi liṃgasyābhyarcanaṃ sakṛt /
ākāśe mahatastasya tejorāśeśca darśanam // 7.2,40.29 //
munīnāṃ vilayaṃ tatra nirodhaṃ tejasastataḥ /
yāthātmyavedanaṃ tasya ciṃtitasyāpi cātmabhiḥ // 7.2,40.30 //
sarvaṃ savistaraṃ tasmai praṇamyāhurmuhurmuhuḥ /
munibhiḥ kathitaṃ śrutvā viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ // 7.2,40.31 //
kaṃpayitvā śiraḥ kiṃcitprāha gaṃbhīrayā girā /
pratyāsīdati yuṣmākaṃ siddhirāmuṣmikī parā // 7.2,40.32 //
bhavadbhirdīrghasatreṇa ciramārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ /
prasādābhimukho bhūta iti bhutārthasūcitam // 7.2,40.33 //
vārāṇasyāṃ tu yuṣmābhiryaddṛṣṭaṃ divi dīptimat /
talliṃgasaṃjñitaṃ sākṣāttejo māheśvaraṃ param // 7.2,40.34 //
tatra līnāśca munayaḥ śrautapāśupatavratāḥ /
muktā babhūvuḥ svasthāśca naiṣṭhikā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ // 7.2,40.35 //
prāpyānena yathā muktiracirādbhavatāmapi /
sa cāyamarthaḥ sūcyeta yuṣmaddṛṣṭena tejasā // 7.2,40.36 //
tatra vaḥ kāla evaiṣa daivādupanataḥ svayam /
prayāta dakṣiṇaṃ meroḥ śikharaṃ devasevitam // 7.2,40.37 //
sanatkumāro yatrāste mama putraḥ paro muniḥ /
pratīkṣyāgamanaṃ sākṣādbhūtanāthasya naṃdinaḥ // 7.2,40.38 //
purā sanatkumāropi dṛṣṭvāpi parameśvaram /
ajñānātsarvayogīndramānī vinayadūṣitaḥ // 7.2,40.39 //
abhyutthānādikaṃ yuktamakurvannatinirbhayaḥ /
tato 'parādhātkruddhena mahoṣṭro naṃdinā kṛtaḥ // 7.2,40.40 //
atha kālena mahatā tadarthe śocatā mayā /
upāsya devaṃ devīñca naṃdinaṃ cānunīya vai // 7.2,40.41 //
kathaṃciduṣṭratā tasya prayatnena nivāritā /
prāpito hi yathāpūrvaṃ sanatpūrvāṃ kumāratām // 7.2,40.42 //
tadāha ca mahādevaḥ smayanniva gaṇādhipam /
avajñāya hi māmeva tathāhaṃkṛtavānmuniḥ // 7.2,40.43 //
atastvameva yāthātmyaṃ mamāsmai kathayānagha /
brahmaṇaḥ pūrvajaḥ putro māṃ mūḍha iva saṃsmaran // 7.2,40.44 //
mayaiva śiṣyate datto mama jñānapravartakaḥ /
dharmādhyakṣābhiṣekaṃ ca tava nirvartayiṣyati // 7.2,40.45 //
sa evaṃ vyāhṛto bhūyassarvabhūtagaṇāgraṇīḥ /
yatparājñāpanaṃ mūrdhnā prātaḥ pratigṛhītavān // 7.2,40.46 //
tathā sanatkumāro 'pi merau madanuśāsanāt /
prasādārthaṃ gaṇasyāsya tapaścarati duścaram // 7.2,40.47 //
draṣṭavyaśceti yuṣmābhiḥ prāggaṇeśasamāgamāt /
tatprasādārthamacirānnaṃdī tatrāgamiṣyati // 7.2,40.48 //
iti satvaramādiśya preṣitā viśvayoginā /
kumāraśikharaṃ merordakṣiṇaṃ munayo yayuḥ // 7.2,40.49 //
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe naimiṣarṣiyātrāvarṇanaṃ nāma catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca /
tatra skaṃdasaro nāma sarassāgarasannibham /
amṛtasvāduśiśirasvacchā gādhalaghūdakam // 7.2,41.1 //
samaṃtataḥ saṃghaṭitaṃ sphaṭiko palasaṃcayaiḥ /
sarvartukusumaiḥ phullaiśchāditākhiladiṅmukham // 7.2,41.2 //
śaivalairutpalaiḥ padmaiḥ kumudaistārakopamaiḥ /
taraṃgairabhrasaṃkāśairākāśamiva bhūmigam // 7.2,41.3 //
sukhāvataraṇārohaiḥ sthalairnīlaśilāmayaiḥ /
sopānamārgau ruciraiśśobhamānāṣṭadiṅmukham // 7.2,41.4 //
tatrāvatīrṇaiśca yathā tatrottīrṇaśca bhūyasā /
snātaiḥ sitopavītaiśca śuklākaupīnavalkalaiḥ // 7.2,41.5 //
jaṭāśikhāyanairmuṃḍaistripuṃḍrakṛtamaṃḍanaiḥ /
virāgavivaśasmeramukhairmunikumārakaiḥ // 7.2,41.6 //
ghaṭaiḥ kamalinīpatrapuṭaiśca kalaśaiḥ śivaiḥ /
kamaṇḍalubhiranyaiśca tādṛśaiḥ karakādibhiḥ // 7.2,41.7 //
ātmārthaṃ ca parārthaṃ ca devatārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ /
ānīyamānasalilamāttapuṣpaṃ ca nityaśaḥ // 7.2,41.8 //
aṃtarjalaśilārūḍhairnīcānāṃ sparśaśaṃkayā /
ācāravadbhirmunibhiḥ kṛtabhasmāṃgadhūsaraiḥ // 7.2,41.9 //
itastato 'psu majjadbhiriṣṭaśiṣṭaiḥ śilāgataiḥ /
tilaiśca sākṣataiḥ puṣpaistyaktadarbhapavitrakaiḥ // 7.2,41.10 //
devādyamṛṣimadhyaṃ ca nirvartya pitṛtarpaṇam /
nivedayedabhijñebhyo nityasnānagatān dvijān // 7.2,41.11 //
sthānesthāne kṛtānekabalipuṣpasamīraṇaiḥ /
saurārghyapūrvaṃ kurvadbhiḥsthaṃḍalebhyarcanādikam // 7.2,41.12 //
kvacinnimajjadunmajjatprasrastagajayūthapam /
kvacicca tṛṣayāyātamṛgīmṛgaturaṃgamam // 7.2,41.13 //
kvacitpītajanottīrṇamayūravaravāraṇam /
kvacitkṛtataṭāghātavṛṣaprativṛṣojjvalam // 7.2,41.14 //
kvacitkāraṃḍavaravaiḥ kvacitsārasakūjitaiḥ /
kvacicca kokaninadaiḥ kvacidbhramaragītibhiḥ // 7.2,41.15 //
snānapānādikaraṇaiḥ svasaṃpaddrumajīvibhiḥ /
praṇayātprāṇibhistaistairbhāṣamāṇamivāsakṛt // 7.2,41.16 //
kūlaśākhiśikhālīnakokilākulakūjitaiḥ /
ātapopahatānsarvānnāmaṃtrayadivāniśam // 7.2,41.17 //
uttare tasya sarasastīre kalpataroradhaḥ /
vedyāṃ vajraśilāmayyāṃ mṛdule mṛgacarmaṇi // 7.2,41.18 //
sanatkumāramāsīnaṃ śaśvadbālavapurdharam /
tatkālamātroparataṃ samādheracalātmanaḥ // 7.2,41.19 //
upāsyamānaṃ munibhiryogīṃdrairapi pūjitam /
dadṛśurnaimiṣeyāste praṇatāścopatasthire // 7.2,41.20 //
yāvatpṛṣṭavate tasmai procuḥ svāgatakāraṇam /
tumulaḥ śuśruve tāvaddivi duṃdubhinisvanaḥ // 7.2,41.21 //
dadṛśe tatkṣaṇe tasminvimānaṃ bhānusannibham /
gaṇeśvarairasaṃkhyeyaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ ca samaṃtataḥ // 7.2,41.22 //
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ rudrakanyābhirāvṛtam /
mṛdaṃgamurajodghuṣṭaṃ veṇuvīṇāravānvitam // 7.2,41.23 //
citraratnavitānāḍhyaṃ muktādāmavirājitam /
munibhissiddhagaṃdharvairyakṣacāraṇakinnaraiḥ // 7.2,41.24 //
nṛtyadbhiścaiva gāyadbhirvādayadbhiśca saṃvṛtam /
vīragovṛṣacihnena vidramadrumayaṣṭinā // 7.2,41.25 //
kṛtagopurasatkāraṃ ketunā mānyahetunā /
tasya madhye vimānasya cāmaradvitayāṃtare // 7.2,41.26 //
chattrasya maṇidaṃḍasya caṃdrasyeva śuceradhaḥ /
divyasiṃhāsanārūḍhaṃ devyā suyaśayā saha // 7.2,41.27 //
śriyā ca vapuṣā caiva tribhiścāpi vilocanaiḥ /
prākārairabhikṛtyānāṃ pratyabhijñāpakaṃ prabhoḥ // 7.2,41.28 //
avilaṃghya jagatkarturājñāpanamivāgatam /
sarvānugrahaṇaṃ śaṃbhoḥ sākṣādiva puraḥsthitam // 7.2,41.29 //
śilādatanayaṃ sākṣācchrīmacchūlavarāyudham /
viśveśvaragaṇādhyakṣaṃ viśveśvaramivāparam // 7.2,41.30 //
viśvasyāpi vidhātḥṇāṃ nigrahānugrahakṣamam /
caturbāhumudārāṃgaṃ candrarekhāvibhūṣitam // 7.2,41.31 //
kaṃṭhe nāgena maulau ca śaśāṃkenāpyalaṃkṛtam /
savigrahamivaiśvaryaṃ sāmarthyamiva sakriyam // 7.2,41.32 //
samāptamiva nirvāṇaṃ sarvajñamiva saṃgatam /
dṛṣṭvā prahṛṣṭavadano brahmaputraḥ saharṣibhiḥ // 7.2,41.33 //
tasthau prāñjalirutthāya tasyātmānamivārpayan /
atha tatrāṃtare tasminvimāne cāvaniṃ gate // 7.2,41.34 //
praṇamya daṇḍavaddevaṃ stutvā vyajñāpayanmunīm /
ṣaṭkulīyā ime dīrghaṃ naimiṣe satram āsthitāḥ /
āgatā brahmaṇādiṣṭāḥ pūrvamevābhikāṃkṣayā // 7.2,41.35 //
śrutvā vākyaṃ brahmaputrasya naṃdīchittvā pāśāndṛṣṭipātena sadyaḥ /
śaivaṃ dharmaṃ caiśvaraṃ jñānayogaṃ dattvā bhūyo devapārśvaṃ jagāma // 7.2,41.36 //
sanatkumāreṇa ca tatsamastaṃ vyāsāya sākṣādgurave mamoktam /
vyāsena coktaṃ mahitena mahyaṃ mayā ca tadvaḥ kathitaṃ samāsāt // 7.2,41.37 //
nāvedavidbhyaḥ kathanīyametatpurāṇaratnaṃ puraśāsanasya /
nābhaktaśiṣyāya ca nāstikebhyo dattaṃ hi mohānnirayaṃ dadāti // 7.2,41.38 //
mārgeṇa sevānugatena yaistaddattaṃ gṛhītaṃ paṭhitaṃ śrutaṃ vā /
tebhyaḥ sukhaṃ dharmamukhaṃ trivargaṃ nirvāṇamaṃte niyataṃ dadāti // 7.2,41.39 //
parasparasyopakṛtaṃ bhavadbhirmayā ca paurāṇikamārgayogāt /
ato gamiṣye 'hamavāptakāmaḥ samastamevāstu śivaṃ sadā naḥ // 7.2,41.40 //
sūte kṛtāśiṣi gate munayaḥ suvṛttā yāge ca paryavasite mahati prayoge /
kāle kalau ca viṣayaiḥ kaluṣāyamāṇe vārāṇasīparisare vasatiṃ vinetuḥ // 7.2,41.41 //
atha ca te paśupāśamumukṣayākhilatayā kṛtapāśupatavratāḥ /
adhikṛtākhilabodhasamādhayaḥ paramanirvṛtimāpuraniṃditāḥ // 7.2,41.42 //
vyāsa uvāca /
etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi samāptaṃ hitamādarāt /
paṭhitavyaṃ prayatnena śrotavyaṃ ca tathaiva hi // 7.2,41.43 //
nāstikāya na vaktavyamaśraddhāya śaṭhāya ca /
abhaktāya maheśasya tathā dharmadhvajāya ca // 7.2,41.44 //
etacchrutyā hyekavāraṃ bhavetpāpaṃ hi bhasmasāt /
abhakto bhaktimāpnoti bhakto bhaktisamṛddhibhāk // 7.2,41.45 //
punaḥ śrute ca sadbhaktirmuktissyācca śruteḥ punaḥ /
tasmātpunaḥpunaścaiva śrotavyaṃ hi mumukṣubhiḥ // 7.2,41.46 //
pañcāvṛttiḥ prakartavyā purāṇasyāsya saddhiyā /
paraṃ phalaṃ samuddiśya tatprāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ // 7.2,41.47 //
purātanāśca rājāno viprā vaiśyāśca sattamāḥ /
saptakṛtvastadāvṛttyālabhanta śivadarśanam // 7.2,41.48 //
śroṣyatyathāpi yaścedaṃ mānavo bhaktitatparaḥ /
iha bhuktvākhilānbhogānaṃte muktiṃ labhecca saḥ // 7.2,41.49 //
etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi śivasyātipriyaṃ param /
bhuktimuktipradaṃ brahmasaṃmitaṃ bhaktivardhanam // 7.2,41.50 //
etacchivapurāṇasya vaktuḥ śrotuśca sarvadā /
sagaṇassasutassāṃbaśśaṃ karotu sa śaṃkaraḥ // 7.2,41.51 //
||oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe vyāsopadeśaśrīśivamahāpurāṇamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ samāpto 'yaṃ granthaḥ
